#
"RACE DARK DWARF"

    This race is one of the evil races of the realms, which
    means that good aligned guards and protectors will attack
    them on sight.  Coming from the Underdark, they have
    infravision, and can be very hardy, gaining a +1 bonus to
    constitution.  However, their stature makes them
    less nimble and have a -1 penalty to dexterity.  Coming from
    the darkness also leaves an imprint on their manners, they
    will never be the most charismatic of individuals.  They tend
    to only focus on a couple roles, see 'help race class combinations'.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 4'
    Average Weight: 140 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 400 years

#
"RACE DROW ELF"

    This race is one of the evil races of the realms, which
    means that good aligned guards and protectors will attack
    them on sight.  Coming from the Underdark, they have
    infravision, and tend to be very agile, gaining a +2 bonus
    to dexterity, but not very hardy, having a -1 penalty to
    constitution.  And the culture of the Underdark means that
    they do not mix well with other people, so are less
    charismatic with a -1 penalty.  They excel in the magic arts,
    see 'help race class combinations' for a complete listing
    of their classes.

    Infravision
    Resist Charm Spells
    Average Height: 4'6"
    Average Weight: 105 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 1500 years

#
"RACE DWARF"

    This race is one of the basic fundamentals of the world.
    The hardy dwarf, who is as sturdy as the mountain, gaining a
    +1 bonus to constitution.  However, being a dwarf also means
    that dexterity suffers from their short stature with a -1
    penalty.  While they have no natural disadvantages for their
    charisma, the general dwarven nature means that they will
    never be as charismatic as is possible for other races.  See
    'help race class combinations' for a complete listing
    of their classes.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 4'
    Average Weight: 140 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 400 years

#
"RACE FOREST GNOME"

    This race is the most common gnome race, with strong ties
    to nature.  Even the elves respect the empathy these
    creatures have with the forest, and they share the gift
    of infravision as well.  Their stature and life
    style lends them to be quick, gaining a +1 bonus to
    dexterity and wise, gaining a +1 bonus to wisdom, but they
    do not pursue the intellectual arts and thus take a -1 penalty
    to their intelligence, nor are interested in being
    the strongest creature of the forest, with a -1 penalty to
    strength.  They tend to gravitate to classes that deal with
    nature, see 'help race class combinations'.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 3'4"
    Average Weight: 103 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 550 years

#
"RACE GOBLIN"

    This race is one of the weaker races, and in many respects
    resembles the halfling race.  Naturally vicious and
    lacking in magic arts, this race is quick and nimble, gaining
    a +1 bonus to dexterity, but lacks the size to be very strong,
    a -1 penalty to strength.  The quickness makes them ideal
    thieves, and their attitude allows them to advance
    quite far as a warrior as well, see 'help race class
    combinations'.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 3'3"
    Average Weight: 50 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 100 years

#
"RACE GOLD ELF"

    This race is one of the sub-races of elves, considered to be
    the elite of the society.  Considered flighty, they have a
    -1 penalty to wisdom and are not very hardy, with a -1 penalty
    to constitution.  However, their intellect when focussed is
    considerable, granting a +1 bonus to intelligence, and are very
    nimble, like most elves, gaining a +1 bonus to dexterity.  While
    they come from the high stratus of elven society, they excel at
    base thievery naturally, and many choose to combine their magical
    arts with the arts of the underworld.  See 'help race class
    combinations' for more details.

    Infravision
    Resist Charm Spells
    Average Height: 4'6"
    Average Weight: 105 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 1500 years

#
"RACE HALF-ELF"

    This race is the result of rare interbreeding between elves
    and humans.  Usually considered out of place in both societies,
    they have lost some of their elven attributes, but gained some
    of the size and hardiness of the human race.  Their upbringing
    gives them a strong sense of character, they make excellent
    rangers and paladins.  However, those that become bitter often
    turn towards thievery.  See 'help race class combinations' for
    more details.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 5'7"
    Average Weight: 125 pounds
    Size Classification: Medium
    Life Span: 300 years

#
"RACE HALF-GIANT"

    This race is one of the largest "civilized" races in the realms.
    While called "Half"-Giant, they are not the product of any
    bizarre mingling of giants and humans.  They are their own race,
    noted for their immensity and physical prowess.  They receive a
    +2 bonus to strength, and a +1 bonus to constitution, but they
    tend to be slow, both physically and mentally, suffering a -1
    penalty to dexterity, intelligence, and wisdom.  With their
    size and strength, they excel at the warrior arts, see 'help
    race class combinations' for more information.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 11'7"
    Average Weight: 1000 pounds
    Size Classification: Huge
    Life Span: 180 years

#
"RACE HALFLING"

    This race is one of the smallest of the realms, noted for their
    lack of moral scruples, but mostly in a light hearted way.
    Exceptionally quick, they receive a +1 bonus to dexterity, but
    also receive a -1 penalty to strength due to their small stature
    and sedentary ways.  While they can do other things, the majority
    of halflings you meet will be thieves of some kind, and usually
    quite skilled at it.  See 'help race class combinations' for more
    details.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 3'4"
    Average Weight: 60 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 180 years

#
"RACE HALF-OGRE"

    This race results from the usually violent unions of ogres and
    humans.  They gain some of the size of their ogre parentage, but
    also the civilizing influences of their human parent.  The size
    grants them a +1 bonus to strength and constitution, but also a
    -1 penalty to dexterity.  The limited brain power of the typical
    ogre is passed down as well, resulting in a -1 to intelligence.
    Overall, the half-ogre makes a powerful warrior, and has some
    understanding of the clerical arts.  See 'help race class
    combinations' for more details.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 8'
    Average Weight: 350 pounds
    Size Classification: Large
    Life Span: 85 years

#
"RACE HALF-ORC"

    This race has both orc and human parents, resulting in a fairly
    ugly, large human-like looking child.  Growing very tall, their
    weight does not quite keep up, resulting in a gangling look.
    Their orc heritage grants a +1 bonus to their constitution, while
    also making them fairly ugly by human standards, creating a -1
    penalty to charisma.  They tend to be decent warriors, mediocre
    clerics and good thieves.  See 'help race class combinations' for
    more details.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 7'6"
    Average Weight: 280 pounds
    Size Classification: Large
    Life Span: 85 years

#
"RACE HUMAN"

    This race is the basis for all other races.  The most numerous
    of the realm, they tend to lack many of the other benefits
    granted to the other races, but make up for it with a vast
    selection of classes and unlimited advancement.  See 'help race
    class combinations' for more details.

    Average Height: 5'11"
    Average Weight: 170 pounds
    Size Classification: Medium
    Life Span: 120 years

#
"RACE MOON-ELF"

    This race is the most numerous of the elves.  They tend to
    enjoy the typical elven benefit of quickness, gaining a +1
    bonus to dexterity, but also the frailness, taking a -1
    penalty to constitution.  They tend towards magic and nature,
    similar to the gold elves in what professions they choose.
    See 'help race class combinations' for more details.

    Infravision
    Resist Charm Spells
    Average Height: 4'6"
    Average Weight: 105 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 1500 years

#
"RACE ORC"

    This race is usually a scourge upon the realms, but
    occasionally an orc decides to leave his or her tribe
    and take up adventuring.  They are sizable, gaining a
    +1 to strength and a +1 bonus to constitution, but also
    ending up with a -2 penalty to charisma due to the fact
    that they are an orc.  Also they have a -1 penalty to
    intelligence, due to their lack of civilization.  They
    don't tend to really be incredibly talented at anything,
    but make decent thieves and barbarians, see 'help race
    class combinations' for more details.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 7'6"
    Average Weight: 320 pounds
    Size Classification: Large
    Life Span: 85 years

#
"RACE ROCK GNOME"

    This race tends to live in mountainous regions, without
    much contact with the outside world.  Despite this, they
    are pleasant companions, but terribly lacking in common
    sense.  They are bright, with a +1 bonus to intelligence
    but don't temper that intelligence with wisdom very often,
    having a -1 penalty to wisdom.  Their magical prowess is
    strong, and even with the wisdom penalty make excellent
    mages and clerics.  See 'help race class combinations' for
    more details.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 3'4"
    Average Weight: 103 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 550 years

#
"RACE SEA ELF"

    This race is rarely seen, but hails from the deep oceans
    of the world.  It is likely the are not considered true
    elves anymore, having adapted so well to the underwater
    environs.  However, they share the look of the surface
    elves, but do not share their quickness.  The constant
    swimming they do has made them stronger than one would
    expect, granting a +1 bonus to strength, but they do
    seem to have the elven characteristic lack of hardiness,
    with a -1 penalty to constitution.  They excel at many
    professions, similar to the surface elves.  See 'help
    race class combinations' for more details.

    Infravision
    Resist Charm Spells
    Water Breathing
    Average Height: 4'6"
    Average Weight: 105 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 900 years

#
"RACE SIZE"

    The sizes of the races you can become make a difference 
    in several aspects of adventuring.  Here is a list of the
    sizes for the races you can choose to become at the start
    of your career as well as the races that you can reincarnate
    into by virtue of the 'reincarnate' spell.

    Avariel         Medium
    Cloud Giant     Huge
    Dark Dwarf      Small
    Deep Gnome      Small
    Drow Elf        Small
    Dwarf           Small
    Fire Giant      Huge
    Forest Gnome    Huge
    Frost Giant     Huge
    Gnoll           Large
    Goblin          Small
    Gold Elf        Small
    Half-Elf        Medium
    Half-Giant      Huge
    Halfling        Small
    Half-Ogre       Large
    Half-Orc        Large
    Hill Giant      Huge
    Human           Medium
    Kangaroo        Medium
    Lizardman       Huge
    Mindflayer      Small
    Moon Elf        Small
    Orc             Large
    Primate         Medium
    Rock Gnome      Small
    Sea Elf         Small
    Storm Giant     Huge
    Troll           Large
    Wild Elf        Small

    The current sizes are:
    Tiny        (Giant Insects, Giant Spiders, less than 3' tall/long)
    Small       (Elves, Dwarves, Mindflayers, Patryns, between 3' and 5' tall)
    Medium      (Humans, Kangaroos, Rakshasa, between 5' and 7' tall)
    Large       (Trolls, Otyughs, Tigers, between 7' and 9' tall)
    Huge        (Half-giants, Giants, Golems, between 9' and 15' tall)
    Gargantuan  (Dragons, Basilisks, larger than 15' tall/long)

#
"RACE TROLL"

    This race is barely on the borderline of being civilized
    enough to be considered an adventuring companion.  The
    troll is not "half"-anything, this is a troll that by
    some miracle manages to be acceptable to society.  However,
    most guards do not see it as such, and will attack any
    troll they come across.  Incredibly lanky, the troll is
    wiry and rubbery, they do not seem to be healthy and strong
    but trolls gain much the same attributes as half-giants.  A
    bonus to strength of +2 and a constitution bonus of +1.  Being
    a troll it is not surprising that they suffer a -1 penalty to
    dexterity, intelligence and wisdom.  They excel at combat and
    actually have a rudimentary faith system that allows them
    mediocre cleric power.  See 'help race class combinations' for
    more details.

    Infravision
    Average Height: 7'11"
    Average Weight: 250 pounds
    Size Classification: Large
    Life Span: 180 years

#
"RACE WILD ELF"

    This race is the elvish race closest to nature.  They do not
    build cities, but rather keep to a tribal lifestyle, constantly
    moving.  A lack of focus on the intellectual arts has given
    them a -1 penalty to wisdom and intelligence, but the harshness
    of their existence gives them a +1 bonus to strength, and they
    have the elven nimbleness in full measure, with a +1 bonus to
    dexterity.  They make excellent druids and warriors.  See 'help
    race class combinations' for more details.

    Infravision
    Resist Charm Spells
    Average Height: 5'4"
    Average Weight: 125 pounds
    Size Classification: Small
    Life Span: 900 years

#
"SHOP BALANCE"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  balance
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting

    This command is used in a bank, and it will show you how many gold
    coins you currently have deposited in the bank.  Other bank commands
    are 'deposit' and 'withdraw'.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You are standing in the bank and wish to check your balance.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> balance
    Havok>  Your balance is 50000.

#
"SHOP BUY"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  buy <obj>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing

    This command is used to purchase an item from a store.  You can
    use a special syntax to purchase a quantity of the same item.
    The syntax is <number>*<obj>, where "number" has to be between
    1 and 9.  So you could "buy 9*bread" to buy nine breads at
    once from a baker.  Other commands used in shops are 'list'
    and 'sell'.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You are standing in a shop and wish to buy a bread.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> buy bread
    Havok>  [the Baker] tells you 'That'll be 15 coins, please.'
            You now have a bread (*1).

    Situation: You are standing in a shop and wish to buy 9 breads.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> buy 9*bread
    Havok>  [the Baker] tells you 'That'll be 135 coins, please.'
            You now have a bread (*9).

#
"SHOP CHECK"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  check
    Positions   :  mounted, standing

    This command is used to see whether you have any mail waiting
    for you at the postmaster.  Normally you will be notified whether
    you have mail, but if you wish to verify that information, you
    can use this command in the presence of the postmaster.  'receive'
    and 'mail' are other postmaster commands.

    Situation: You are standing in the same room as the postmaster and
    want to verify that you have no mail.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> check
    Havok>  the postmaster tells you, 'Sorry, you DON'T have any messages
            waiting.'

#
"SHOP DEPOSIT"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  deposit <number>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting

    This command is used in a bank to deposit money into your account.
    You can't deposit more money than you are currently carrying.  The
    other commands a bank will allow is 'balance' and 'withdraw'.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You are standing in the bank and wish to deposit some gold.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> deposit 50000
    Havok>  Thank you.
            Your balance is 100000.

#
"SHOP LIST"

    If you are looking for the list of shop topics try "shop list topics".

    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  list
    Positions   :  mounted, standing

    This command is used in a shop to give you a list of what is available
    to purchase in that shop.  Some shops have unlimited inventory, and some
    have only a few of an item.  The other commands used in stores are 'buy'
    and 'sell'.  The format of the information returned by the list command
    is determined by the individual store.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You are standing in a store and wish to see what they offer
    for sale.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> list
    Havok>  A long sword for 2599 gold coins.
            A wooden club for 12 gold coins.
            A warhammer for 51 gold coins.
            A short bow for 129 gold coins.


#
"SHOP MAIL"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  mail <player>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing

    This command is used in the presence of a postmaster to send
    a mail to any player, whether they are online or offline.  Very
    useful for leaving a message behind to somebody, or to share a
    large amount of information.  It will cost you a nominal amount,
    but the next time the player logs in, they will know that they
    have mail waiting for them.  Other commands are 'check' and
    'receive'.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You are standing at the postmaster and wish to leave a letter
    to your friend Joe.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> mail Joe
    Havok>  The scribe tells you, 'I'll take 150 coins for the delivery.'
            The scribe tells you, 'Write your message, use /w when done.
            Use /? for more info on editing strings.'

#
"SHOP OFFER"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  offer
    Positions   :  mounted, standing

    This command is used to check and see how much rent you will owe
    if you decided to rent.  It will also let you know which items
    can not be rented, and if you have equipment that is inappropriate
    for your character.  You should do this before you rent, so that
    you aren't shocked by your rent bill.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You are ready to leave the mud for a while and are preparing
    to rent out at an inn.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> offer
    Havok>                      a Cubs hat : 11000 coins/day
                               khaki pants : 0 coins/day
                                   sandals : 0 coins/day
                                 a T-shirt : 0 coins/day
            Rosetta the receptionist winks at you and offers you a 5%
            discount. (555 coins)
            [Rosetta the receptionist] tells you 'It will cost you 10544
            coins per day.'
            [Rosetta the receptionist] tells you 'You can stay for 41 days'
            [Rosetta the receptionist] tells you 'You carry 1 rare
            item.'

#
"SHOP RECEIVE"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  receive
    Positions   :  mounted, standing

    This command is used to pick up your mail at the scribe or the postmaster.
    The mud will usually notify you when you have mail waiting and this
    command will get you that mail if you type it in the presence of the
    postmaster.  Then you can 'read' your mail.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You have some mail and you want to get it so you can read it.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> receive
    Havok>  the scribe gives you a piece of mail.

#
"SHOP RENT"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  rent
    Positions   :  mounted, standing

    This command is one of the most important commands.  Using this
    command at an inn, where a receptionist awaits you will allow you
    to leave the game, while saving all your equipment.  This is the
    only safe way to quit the game.  The cost of renting out will be
    displayed to you, if you have a lot of rare or expensive gear you
    might not be able to rent until you have reduced your equipment
    list.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You are ready to leave the mud for a while and have found
    an inn with a receptionist.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> rent
    Havok>                      a Cubs hat : 11000 coins/day
                               khaki pants : 0 coins/day
                                   sandals : 0 coins/day
                                 a T-shirt : 0 coins/day
            Rosetta the receptionist winks at you and offers you a 5%
            discount. (555 coins)
            [Rosetta the receptionist] tells you 'It will cost you 10544
            coins per day.'
            [Rosetta the receptionist] tells you 'You can stay for 41 days'
            [Rosetta the receptionist] tells you 'You carry 1 rare
            item.'
            Rosetta the receptionist stores your stuff in the safe, and helps
            you into your chamber.

            Welcome to -=Havok MUD=-

            0) Exit from Havok Mud.
            1) Enter the game at Karsynia
            2) Enter description.
            3) Read the background story
            4) Change password.
            K) Kill this character!

               Make your choice:

#
"SHOP SELL"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  sell <obj>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing

    This command can be used in a store to sell an item from your inventory
    to the storekeeper.  Storekeepers usually only buy certain types of
    items and they might not have enough money to purchase really expensive
    items.  Other commands used are 'list' and 'buy'.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You have an extra dagger you want to sell to the weapons
    shopkeeper.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> sell dagger
    Havok>  You just sold a dagger for 10 coins.

#
"SHOP SELL"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  value <obj>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing

    This command can be used in some stores to get the price that a
    shopkeeper would purchase an item from you for.  Useful if you
    are not sure if you want to sell an item or not.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You have an extra dagger you want to sell to the weapons
    shopkeeper.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> value dagger
    Havok>  the shopkeeper tells you 'I'll give you 10 gold coins for that!'

#
"SHOP WITHDRAW"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  withdraw <number>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting

    This command is used in a bank to take out some of your saved
    gold.  You can not withdraw more gold than you have stored in the
    bank.

    (Situation, what you type at the prompt, the message you should see):
    Situation: You are standing in the bank and wish to take out some gold.
    H:50/50 M:120/120 V:100/100> withdraw 50000
    Havok>  Thank you.
            Your balance is 50000.

#
"SKILL ADRENALIZE"
    Usable by   :  psi 20
    Usage       :  adrenalize <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  15

    This skill is used by the psionist to send the target creature into a
    barely controlled frenzied state.  It will boost the strength of the
    target, and make them hit harder at the cost of losing some accuracy.
    It lasts for a handful of hours.

#
"SKILL AURA"
    Usable by   :  psi 5
    Usage       :  aura
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  40

    This skill is used by the psionist to allow him or her to see the
    auras of the creatures he or she encounters.  Magical auras and
    the morality auras become visible to the naked eye.  A white aura
    surrounding an individual means they are basically good in nature,
    while a red aura means they are evil.  A blue aura will surround
    any magical item.  No aura would indicate that the creature doesn't
    lean towards good or evil.  This can last a very long time, over
    four days if the psionist is very powerful.

#
"SKILL AVOID BACKATTACK"
    Usable by  :  barb 1
    Usage      :  -
    Positions  :  standing, fighting
    Speed      :  -
    Mana       :  0

    This skill allows a barbarian to avoid the sneaky backstab of
    a thief.  The preternatural senses of the barbarians can make
    a thief scream in frustration.  Eventually, the barbarian will
    become so adept at this as to make the backstab useless against
    him or her.

#
"SKILL BACKSTAB"
    Usable by   :  thief 1,
    Usage       :  backstab <mob>
    Positions   :  standing
    Speed       :  Single Class Thief: Medium
                   Multi-Class Thief: Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is the primary combat tactic of the thief.  Attacking
    by surprise from behind, the thief can inflict a hideous amount
    of damage in one blow.  However, once the attack has happened,
    the thief then fights like any other fighter.  The thief must
    be wielding a piercing weapon of some kind, a dagger is the
    usual object of choice.  The thief can not backstab somebody
    who is much bigger than they are, and will have a hard time
    backstabbing somebody if there is a lot of fighting going on
    around the target.

#
"SKILL BASH"
    Usable by   :  warrior 1, ranger 1, pal 1, barb 1
    Usage       :  bash [<mob>]
    Positions   :  standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Varies
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is the primary combat tactic of the fighting classes.
    By rushing forward and slamming an opponent to the ground, the
    fighter can stun the opponent for a brief period of time.  While
    stunned, the opponent can not undertake any actions and will
    suffer slightly more damage than if they were standing.  Until
    the opponent stands up again, there are very few actions they
    can effectively pursue.  If there are many people fighting close 
    to the target the fighter will have a hard time getting close 
    enough to bash the target.  If there is no target specified, 
    the fighter will bash the current opponent.  Any size fighter
    can attempt to bash any size opponent.  Large size differentials
    between the fighter and his or her target reduces the chance
    of succeeding at the bash.  If a small fighter, like a dwarf,
    attempted to bash a large target, like a giant, it will be much
    harder than a half-giant attempting to bash the giant.  Likewise,
    a half-giant will have a hard time bashing a goblin.  Being 
    slightly larger than your opponent grants the best chance to
    successfully bash them, so a human attempting to bash a moon-elf
    will have the easiest time.  The level difference between the
    basher and the target will make a difference, so will being
    a single-class, main-class, or a multi-class fighter, as well
    as dexterity.  So the absolutely best opportunity is for a high 
    level, single class fighter with a high dexterity who is one size 
    larger than the target.  The time that the bash stuns the basher 
    and the victim is determined by how successful the bash was and 
    the strength of the basher.

#
"SKILL BELLOW"
    Usable by   :  warrior 1, barb 1
    Usage       :  bellow
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  15

    This skill is used to startle the other creatures in the room.
    There is a chance that the bellow will stun an opponent, or
    make them flee.  If the opponent is made of sterner stuff, they
    will merely get mad at the bellower.  If a single class warrior
    does the bellow, it will act like a 'bash' on all the opponents.

#
"SKILL BERSERK"
    Usable by   :  barb 1
    Usage       :  berserk
    Positions   :  fighting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  15

    This skill is the primary combat skill of the barbarian.  With
    this skill the barbarian launches himself into a incredible
    whirlwind of destruction while already fighting.  He or she gets
    more attacks and hits much harder.  His or her aim suffers a
    little, and he or she can't possibly think of anything as weak
    as retreating, but in the meantime, the destructive ability is
    unparalleled.

#
"SKILL PSIONIC BLAST"
    Usable by   :  psi 1
    Usage       :  blast [<mob>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  25

    This skill is the primary combat skill of psionists.  A basic mental
    assault to the target, it will scramble the brains, causing physical
    damage.  At higher levels, the psionist can severely impair the combat
    abilities of a target.  At the pinnacle of psionist power, the target
    could even end up a vegetable, unable to even try to fight back.

#
"SKILL BLESSING"
    Usable by   :  pal 1
    Usage       :  blessing <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  level * 2

    This skill is a special set of powers, only granted by the paladin's
    deity once every three days.  The higher level the paladin and the
    more pure the target creature, the greater the blessing bestowed.
    At a very minimum the target will receive the basic low level cleric
    spells, such as 'bless' and 'armor'.  As the power of the blessing grows
    so does it's effects, which are cumulative, the most powerful blessings
    will grant multiple 'heal' spells and a 'sanctuary' spell.

#
"SKILL BREW"
    Usable by   :  sorc 1, mage 1
    Usage       :  brew '<spell>'
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  normal cost of spell * 2

    This skill allows a mage or a sorcerer to create a potion of some
    spell that he or she already is able to cast.  Not all spells are
    able to be brewed, and the cost of the brewed spell is twice the
    normal cost of the spell.  If the potion is created successfully,
    then the potion can be quaffed by anybody to receive the effect
    of the spell.

#
"SKILL BS"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  bs <mob>
    Positions   :  standing
    Speed       :  Single Class Thief: Medium
                   Multi-Class Thief: Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is the primary combat tactic of the thief.  Attacking
    by surprise from behind, the thief can inflict a hideous amount
    of damage in one blow.  However, once the attack has happened,
    the thief then fights like any other fighter.  The thief must
    be wielding a piercing weapon of some kind, a dagger is the
    usual object of choice.  The thief can not backstab somebody
    who is much bigger than they are, and will have a hard time
    backstabbing somebody if there is a lot of fighting going on
    around the target.

#
"SKILL CALL STEED"
    Usable by   :  pal 11
    Usage       :  call steed
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill can be used by a paladin to bring a faithful mount
    to his side, able to be ridden outdoors and save the paladin
    strength to fight.  You automatically 'mount' the horse that
    arrives, and it will obey your commands while you ride it.
    If you don't wish to ride it any more you can 'dismount' it
    and it will remain where it is for you to come back.  The horse
    will obey your orders while you ride it, and aid you in combat.

#
"SKILL CAMOUFLAGE"
    Usable by   :  barb 1
    Usage       :  camouflage
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is used by barbarians to hide in the outdoors, so that
    the only way someone can even know he or she is there is by having
    the spell 'sense life' active.  Being hidden means that you can not
    be targeted except by an opponent with both the 'sense life' and
    the 'true sight' spells.  Area effect spells can still cause you
    damage however.  Any activity will cancel out your hiding, and make
    you visible to all.

#
"SKILL CANIBALIZE"
    Usable by   :  psi 2
    Usage       :  canibalize <amount of hitpoints>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is a great boon to a psionist.  By specifying a number
    of hitpoints after the command, the psionist can change hitpoints
    into mana.  The number of mana points gained is twice as many
    hitpoints.  So if you "canibalize 10" you would receive 20 mana
    points.  You should be careful not to drain your life down so low
    that you are in danger from physical attacks.  If you fail to
    successfully canibalize the health, it is gone with no benefit.

#
"SKILL CARVE"
    Usable by   :  ranger 1
    Usage       :  carve <corpse obj>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  5 if fail

    This skill is known only to the ranger, and is the ability to
    create food out of the carcass of a corpse.  The corpse must
    be of a size able to support this activity, a butterfly is
    not going to make a good ration, but a dragon might provide
    days worth of meals.

#
"SKILL CAST"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  cast '<spell>' [<target>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting
    Speed       :  Determined by spell cast
    Mana        :  Determined by spell cast

    This skill is the basic skill that allows for magic spells to be
    cast.  It only provides access to magic, the spells themselves
    determine all aspects of what happens.  You are either able to
    cast spells or not, there is no "learning" of the cast skill.
    See the individual help of the spell in question to learn what
    it does and how it behaves.

#
"SKILL CHARGE"
    Usable by   :  pal 4,
    Usage       :  charge <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill allows a paladin and his or her mount to become a single
    deadly force, initiating combat with a devastating attack.  While
    riding a mount, the paladin, who must be wielding a weapon that does
    impale damage, rams into the target creature, inflicting terrible
    damage.

#
"SKILL CLIMB"
    Usable by   :  thief 1, ranger 1, barb 1,
    Usage       :  climb <north | east | south | west | up | down>
    Positions   :  standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is used as a substitute to flying in certain places.
    If the way out of a room is marked as a climbable exit, then
    this skill can be used to scale the way across.  Obviously if
    the exit you wish to go to is in midair, then there is no
    way to climb to it.  Be careful, a slip here and you could fall
    quite a ways and possibly be gravely injured.

#
"SKILL DISARM"
    Usable by   :  thief 1, ranger 1, pal 1, monk 1, barb 1, warrior 1
    Usage       :  disarm <trap obj | mob>
    Positions   :  standing, fighting
    Speed       :  For disarming traps: Fast
                   For disarming mobs: Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is used in two ways.  The first is only learned by
    thieves, and that is to disarm deadly traps.  The other is
    used by fighters to disarm an opponent.  Monks are more proficient
    at this maneuver than other fighters.  If successful the weapon
    of the opponent is sent flying from his or her hand and they are
    forced to fight bare handed unless they can retrieve the weapon or
    wield a new weapon.  Something to keep in mind is that many
    creatures do devastating damage with their bare fists and the
    weapon they wield makes little difference in the level of danger
    they represent.

#
"SKILL DISENGAGE"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  disengage [<-skill>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill can be learned to back out of combat without having to
    flee madly from the room.  Using the "-skill" argument will tell
    you how well you have learned this skill and using the command
    without any argument while fighting will cause you to stop
    fighting if successful.  If you are the tank for a fight and
    attempt this, chances are the opponent will start hitting you
    again as soon as he or she can.

#
"SKILL DISGUISE"
    Usable by   :  barb 1, thief 1
    Usage       :  disguise
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill gives you the ability to hide from any people who might
    hate you.  This skill, which can only be used once a day, will
    keep you safe from somebody you have been fighting with earlier.
    They will not recognize you and will not attack you, unless they
    would normally attack you by being 'aggressive'.

#
"SKILL DOORBASH"
    Usable by   :  warrior 1, ranger 1, barb 1
    Usage       :  doorbash <door name> [<north | east | south | west |
                   up | down>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill costs nothing in mana, but it does cost some movement
    points, which is logical given that this skill is nothing besides
    throwing ones shoulder against a door in an attempt to open it.
    Some doors can not be forced no matter what and will need a key.
    If you are clumsy in attempting this maneuver, you will end up
    stumbling through the door into the next room.  If you fail to
    open a door, you will find yourself stunned, with a ringing head
    and a bruised shoulder.

#
"SKILL DOORWAY"
    Usable by   :  psi 3
    Usage       :  doorway <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  20

    This skill is a defining ability of the psionist mental powers.
    Using this skill, a psionist can instantly transport him or herself
    to another creature.  The travel is cheap, fast, and comes at a very
    low level.  It is the first step to the powerful transportation magics
    available to a psionist.

#
"SKILL ESP"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  esp
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  10

    This skill helps a psionist to understand every type of language,
    simply bypassing the words and looking at the thoughts.  It doesn't
    do anything to help the psionist speak any language, but at least
    he or she can understand anybody while the skill lasts, which may
    be as long as a day at the highest level of ability.

#
"SKILL FEIGN DEATH"
    Usable by   :  monk 1
    Usage       :  feign death
    Positions   :  fighting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is only able to be achieved by monks without the aid of
    magic.  If successful, the monk will immediately pretend to be
    struck down fatally in combat.  The opponents being thus fooled
    will stop fighting, leaving the monk free to recover.  If the monk
    is very good at this skill, he or she might not even be noticed
    anymore, being hidden in plain sight as a corpse.

#
"SKILL FIND FOOD"
    Usable by   :  barb 1, ranger 1
    Usage       :  find food
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill enables you to scrounge up a handful of berries as
    sustenance in the outdoors.  It is a slow, tedious process and
    has no chance of working indoors.  It is rumored that there
    is a way for anybody to learn these skills.

#
"SKILL FIND TRAP"
    Usable by   :  thief 1
    Usage       :
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill, learnable by thieves, gives an almost supernatural
    ability to detect the presence of traps, which are invisible
    to the naked eye.  It requires no particular concentration
    on the part of the thief, the traps are visible to him or
    her just like any other object of a room.  The majority of
    traps are triggered by disturbing them by touching them or
    by attempting to move past them.

#
"SKILL FIND WATER"
    Usable by   :  barb 1, ranger 1
    Usage       :  find water
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill enables you to scrounge up a cupful of water as
    sustenance in the outdoors.  It is a slow, tedious process and
    has no chance of working indoors.  It is rumored that there
    is a way for anybody to learn these skills.

#
"SKILL FIRST AID"
    Usable by   :  ranger 1, barb 1,
    Usage       :  first aid
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill, usable once per day, provides a quick boost of
    healing to the ranger or barbarian.  The amount of healing
    is determined by the level of the character.

#
"SKILL FLAME SHROUD"
    Usable by   :  psi 15
    Usage       :  flame
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  40

    This skill gives the psionist the power to summon flames, like
    the 'fireshield' spell around his body.  This skill lasts much
    longer than the 'fireshield' spell, and as long as it lasts, if
    anybody hits the psionist, the shroud will scorch them with fire.

#
"SKILL FLOWERFIST"
    Usable by   :  monk 36
    Usage       :  flowerfist
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is not that impressive in terms of damage, but the
    very fact that an unarmed fighter is able to cause damage to
    multiple opponents at once is impressive enough.  It deals
    between 6 and 36 points of damage to as many as 7 opponents.
    This damage comes from focussing the chi to allow a brief moment
    where the monk's punching fist is actually in several places at
    once.

#
"SKILL FLURRY"
    Usable by   :  monk 18
    Usage       :  flurry
    Positions   :  fighting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is a powerful combat maneuver, that only masters
    of the martial arts can even attempt.  By focussing the chi,
    the monk can make combat seem to move more slowly, giving
    him more attacks and a better chance of hitting his opponents.
    It only lasts for one round of combat, and after that you
    have to recover for a bit before trying again.

#
"SKILL GREAT SIGHT"
    Usable by   :  psi 11
    Usage       :  great
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  50

    This skill grants the psionist a great deal of detection abilities
    in one skill.  Using this will grant the psionist the same effects
    as the spells 'true sight', 'sense life' and 'detect invisibility'.
    The amount of time all the effects last is different for each effect,
    but the more powerful the psionist, the longer the effect lasts.

#
"SKILL HEROIC RESCUE"
    Usable by   :  pal 1
    Usage       :  heroic
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is a great boon to a paladin, especially one traveling
    with weaker companions.  Acting much like the 'rescue' skill, it
    allows the paladin to step in between his or her companion and
    the dangerous opponents they were fighting.  It is considered
    significantly superior to the 'rescue' skill in the fact that
    no target has to be specified.  This is because the 'heroic
    rescue' skill will automatically rescue all members of your group
    from combat.  If you have 3 group members fighting 2 different
    opponents, doing a 'heroic rescue' will mean that the 2 group
    members who were being attacked by the opponents will be rescued
    from the combat and you will now be getting attacked by both of the
    opponents they were fighting.  Essentially, the paladin will be
    throwing himself in between his or her companions and any opponent
    of the group.

#
"SKILL HIDE"
    Usable by   :  thief 1, ranger 2, monk 1
    Usage       :  hide
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill can be very useful to the thief, monk, and ranger
    in certain circumstances.  The ranger can only use this ability
    outside, but the monk and thief can use it anywhere.  If you
    successfully hide, you will be almost completely undetectable.
    Without the 'sense life' spell or ability, any other creature
    will have no idea that you are even present in the room.  Without
    'sense life' and 'true sight' you can not even be targeted by
    another creature.  However, the moment you take any action, you
    will no longer be considered hiding and can be spotted by anybody
    who would normally be able to see you.

#
"SKILL HUNT"
    Usable by   :  barb 1, ranger 1, thief 1
    Usage       :  track <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is very useful, and can be mimicked by the spells 'minor
    track' and 'major track'.  It allows the barbarian or ranger to
    track down a particular creature.  While not all creatures can
    be tracked, the more skilled you are at hunting, the farther
    away the target can be and still be tracked.  You are slowed down
    while you track your quarry.

#
"SKILL HYPNOTIZE"
    Usable by   :  psi 2
    Usage       :  hypnotize <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  25

    This skill is used by a psionist to overwhelm the mind of another
    creature and force it do his or her bidding.  If a creature is
    extraordinarily stupid, it is impossible to create a mental
    connection to it.  If successful, the creature will obey your
    every 'order' for the next day and a half.

#
"SKILL ID"
    Usable by   :  mage 10, sorc 10, cleric 16
    Usage       :  id <obj>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  15

    This skill is actually just a short cut to casting the 'identify'
    spell.  Thus, you must be able to cast the 'identify' spell for
    this "skill" to work.

#
"SKILL KICK"
    Usable by   :  warrior 1, monk 1
    Usage       :  kick [<mob>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is a combat maneuver, if used while fighting without
    specifying a target, your current opponent will be the target.
    Monks are much better than a warrior at this action, but it
    takes both of them a long time to recover.

#
"SKILL LAY ON HANDS"
    Usable by   :  pal 1
    Usage       :  lay on hands <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is a powerful one shot healing ability of the paladin.
    Once per day, the paladin can lay hands on another person, healing
    them of damage.  The more powerful the paladin, the greater the
    healing, and if the target is pure enough to be a paladin themselves,
    the healing is doubled.

#
"SKILL LEGSWEEP"
    Usable by   :  monk 1
    Usage       :  legsweep [<mob>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is the monk's equivalent of the 'bash' skill for
    fighters.  If successful the monk will knock the target down
    to the ground, temporarily stunning them.  The monk also needs
    time to recover from the attack.  If all goes well the monk
    will be ready to legsweep the opponent again when the opponent
    finally starts to stand up.  If no target is specified then
    the current opponent will be targeted.

#
"SKILL MEDITATE"
    Usable by   :  psi 1
    Usage       :  meditate
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is available to psionists to place themselves into
    a rejuvenating trance.  While meditating, which is a position
    similar to resting, the psionist will recover mana faster than
    if he or she were just resting.  Probably not as fast as sleeping
    but the psionist is still aware of all that happens around him
    or her while meditating.

#
"SKILL MEMORIZE"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  memorize '<spell>'
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Depends on Spell
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is used by sorcerers to memorize spells so that later
    they can 'recall' them.  Instead of using mana to power any
    spell, the sorcerer commits a particular spell to memory, then
    instead of using 'cast' to launch a spell, the sorcerer uses
    'recall' to launch the spell.  However, once the sorcerer has
    successfully memorized a spell, he or she can recall it perfectly,
    there is no chance of the spell failing.  Low power spells, memorized
    by a very intelligent high level sorcerer takes practically no time
    at all.  However, a very powerful spell that is just at the edge of
    your ability to cast will take much longer.

#
"SKILL MEND"
    Usable by   :  warrior 1
    Usage       :  mend <obj>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill, which is available only to warriors, allows a warrior
    to fix damaged gear.  Failure means that the equipment is actually
    worse off than it was before the attempted mending, but success
    brings the gear back to full strength, even weapons.

#
"SKILL MESSENGER"
    Usable by   :  cleric 1, druid 1
    Usage       :  messenger <mob> <message>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  5

    This skill allows a cleric or druid to send a private message to
    anybody in the realm.  Nobody but the user and the target know
    what is said, or even that anything was said.  This is similar
    to a global 'tell' command.

#
"SKILL MIND"
    Usable by   :  psi 1
    Usage       :  mind '<power>'
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting
    Speed       :  Depends on skill called
    Mana        :  Depends on skill called

    This skill is the psionist equivalent to the 'cast' command.
    The psionist accesses his powers throw this command, see the
    different powers (which are found under "help mind <power>")
    to find the specific details.

#
"SKILL PICK"
    Usable by   :  thief 1
    Usage       :  pick <door name>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill allows a thief to unlock a door without a key.
    Not all doors can be unlocked in this manner, some require
    a key no matter what you attempt to do to the door.

#
"SKILL PSI PORTAL"
    Usable by   :  psi 32
    Usage       :  portal <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  50

    This skill is one of the psionists more expensive powers, but
    very useful in a group.  When successfully used, this power
    opens a brief portal to the target, and every companion of
    the psionist steps through it, appearing instantly at the
    target's location.

#
"SKILL PSIONIC INVISIBILITY"
    Usable by   :  psi 1
    Usage       :  psionic invisibility
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  10

    This skill allows the psionist to briefly contact the minds of
    the creatures he or she encounters.  In that brief moment, the
    psionist convinces the creature that he or she is not there.
    When a creature looks to where the psionist is, their brain
    refuses to acknowledge what is in front of them.  However, due
    to the magical way that the 'detect invisibility' spell works,
    it will show the truth of even an invisible psionist.  Any
    attack will dispel the invisibility automatically, and it can
    be cancelled manually by using the 'vis' command.  The longest
    this power can be maintained is a day.

#
"SKILL QUIVERING PALM"
    Usable by   :  monk 30
    Usage       :  quivering palm [<mob>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is the most terrifying ability of the monk.  By
    concentrating chi into the hand, and a near perfect knowledge
    of physical and spiritual anatomy, the monk can set up
    deadly vibrations in the body and soul of an opponent.  If
    successful, the opponent will likely drop dead, due to an
    interruption in the flow of blood and chi.  If an opponent
    is more powerful than you, or has a great deal more hitpoints,
    then this skill will be ineffectual against them.  This
    devastating ability is so draining that it can only be
    performed once a week.

#
"SKILL RECALL"
    Usable by   :  sorc 1
    Usage       :  recall '<spell>' [<target>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting
    Speed       :  Depends on spell
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is only used by the sorcerer, and it replaces
    the 'cast' command for launching spells.  If the sorcerer
    has a spell memorized, this command will release it and
    the effects are determined by which spell it is.  This
    command can never fail, if the spell has been memorized,
    recalling it is flawless.

#
"SKILL RECALLHOME"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  recallhome
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is most useful for low level characters.  Provided
    that you are on the same plane as your home town (the inn where
    you last rented), this command will return you to that place.
    However, it is not a sure thing, your chances of successfully
    recalling decrease as your level increases.  Your percentage
    of successfully doing it ranges from 100% as a brand new
    character to 2% as a powerful hero.  If you do use the command
    successfully, you will be instantly returned, but your movement
    will have been drained to 0.

#
"SKILL RECITE"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  recite <scroll> [<target>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is used to cast the magic from a scroll.  The scroll
    will burst into flames, so it is not reusable, and the target
    of the scroll will be the target of whatever spells are released.

#
"SKILL RESCUE"
    Usable by   :  warrior 1, ranger 3
    Usage       :  rescue <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is used to rescue one person who is currently getting
    beat up by an opponent.  If successful, the target is removed
    from combat with that opponent, but other opponents can still
    continue to attack the target.  The target will be temporarily
    stunned by the rescue and won't be able to initiate new actions
    until he or she recovers.

#
"SKILL RETREAT"
    Usable by   :  thief 1, monk 1, barb 1
    Usage       :  retreat
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is not a separate ability, but is built in to
    the 'flee' command.  You can use the 'retreat' command, but
    it merely calls the 'flee' command.  If you succeed in your
    retreat skill, you will not flee blindly and not lose
    experience for running away.  It merely turns what was
    a panicky maneuver into one that has some order to it.

#
"SKILL RIDE"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  ride <rideable mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill doubles as both a learnable skill "riding" that
    helps you to control your animal when mounted, and it also
    will perform the 'mount' command.  If you have learned the
    riding skill well, you will fall off your mount far less
    often than if you have not learned anything about it, which
    can be a big difference if you plan on fighting from the
    back of your mount.

#
"SKILL SCRIBE"
    Usable by   :  cleric 1
    Usage       :  scribe '<spell>'
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  Depends on spell

    This skill is used by clerics to make a scroll that has a
    spell imbued on it.  The spell is decided by the cleric,
    and it costs twice as much mana to put it on a scroll as
    it does to cast it normally.  The scroll has a limited
    shelf life, it's not stable and will dissolve in a matter
    of hours.  The scroll can be recited just like any other
    scroll.  Not all spells are able to be scribed onto a
    scroll, check the individual spell help to see if that
    spell can be scribed.

#
"SKILL SCRY"
    Usable by   :  psi 7
    Usage       :  scry <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  20

    This skill is used by a psionist to view the location of a
    target creature.  Any target in the world can be viewed,
    provided they aren't protected somehow.

#
"SKILL SENDING"
    Usable by   :  ranger 1, mage 1, sorc 1
    Usage       :  sending <mob> <message>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  5

    This skill allows a mage, sorcerer or ranger to send a private
    message to anybody in the realm.  Nobody but the user and the
    target know what is said, or even that anything was said.  This
    is similar to a global 'tell' command.

#
"SKILL PSI SHIELD"
    Usable by   :  psi 1
    Usage       :  shield
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  10

    This skill is a simple piece of unconscious telekinesis that provides
    a barrier between the psionist and harm.  It can only push away
    physical threats, so it protects against the psionist in combat.  The
    barrier grows stronger as the psionist gets stronger, eventually
    protecting better than any armor ever crafted.

#
"SKILL SNEAK"
    Usable by   :  thief 1, ranger 4, monk 1
    Usage       :  sneak
    Positions   :  standing
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill allows the character to walk around without being noticed
    by anybody.  It will slow down your travelling, since you must take
    more care with your steps, but if successful,  you will be able
    to sneak past almost any creature.  However, in order to sneak about,
    you can not be wearing any item that makes noise, such as a powerful
    magic item that hums.  Rangers can not sneak indoors, only outdoors,
    so this skill has limited use for them in urban settings.

#
"SKILL SPOT"
    Usable by   :  ranger 3, pal 1, warrior 1, barb 1
    Usage       :  spot [<north | east | south | west | up | down>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Spotting in a direction: Medium
                   Spotting all around: Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill allows you to look around and scan for other creatures
    nearby.  Only the paladin and the ranger can learn this skill from
    their guildmasters.  But there is another teacher of this skill that
    any fighter can learn from.  You can not spot any creatures that you
    normally wouldn't be able to see anyway, such as hidden creatures,
    or invisible creatures.  Spotting in a direction will narrow your
    focus, which can be useful in crowded areas.

#
"SKILL SPRING LEAP"
    Usable by   :  monk 1
    Usage       :  springleap [<mob>]
    Positions   :  sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill can be a significant advantage in combat for a monk.
    If the monk is somehow knocked from his feet during combat, he
    can leap off the ground in a tremendous move, driving both feet
    into his or her opponent.  The effect of this is to stun the
    opponent for a short time while doing some damage to the opponent
    and to regain your feet, so that you are standing and ready to
    continue the fight.

#
"SKILL SPY"
    Usable by   :  thief 1, ranger 1, barb 1
    Usage       :  spy
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill allows a person to peer into the next room over by
    using the 'look' command with a direction argument.  If this
    skill is successful, you will see into the next room exactly
    as though you were there.  Very useful for looking before
    leaping.

#
"SKILL STEAL"
    Usable by   :  thief 1
    Usage       :  steal <coins | obj> <mob>
    Positions   :  standing
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill allows a thief to steal gold from another creature,
    provided that creature has some gold.  Also if the target
    has some items in his or her inventory, then they can be
    stolen as well.  Of course the possibility exists that you
    might fail and get caught, but that is the risk that all
    thieves will take.

#
"SKILL PSI SUMMON"
    Usable by   :  psi 15
    Usage       :  summon <mob>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  30

    This skill is very useful to the psionist.  By focussing on the target,
    the psionist can create a portal wherever the target is, and move the
    portal around the creature.  This is the opposite of how the psionist
    uses the 'doorway' skill.  Instead of making a portal from him or
    herself to the target, the psionist makes a portal at the target and
    brings the target to him or her.  The target is not prepared for this
    and will likely be disoriented by the trip.  You can not summon
    creatures who are more powerful than you, and this portal can only
    work on the same plane of existence.  Sometimes the target will be
    protected from this type of ability through magic.  This skill is
    different from the 'summon' spell that mages, sorcerers, and clerics
    receive.  Sometimes the spell will be blocked, while this ability
    can reach the target.

#
"SKILL SWIM"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  swim
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  0

    This skill can be used to temporarily allow yourself to swim underwater.
    For a short duration, you will be able to be underwater, but when you
    can't hold your breath any longer, you better be in an air filled room.

#
"SKILL TAN"
    Usable by   :  ranger 1
    Usage       :  tan <corpse obj> <shield | jacket | boots | gloves |
                   leggings | sleeves | helmet | bag>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing
    Speed       :  Medium
    Mana        :  0

    This skill allows a ranger to skin a corpse for the hide, in order
    to make one of several items out of it.  The more powerful the
    creature, the more effective the armor.

#
"SKILL TELEPATHY"
    Usable by   :  All 1
    Usage       :  telepathy <mob> <message>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Fast
    Mana        :  5

    This skill allows a psionist to send a private and discreet
    message to anybody in the realm.  Nobody but the user and the
    target know what is said, or even that anything was said.  This
    is similar to a global 'tell' command.

#
"SKILL VALUE ITEM"
    Usable by   :  thief 1
    Usage       :  value [<mob>] <obj>
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting, sitting, resting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is the ability of the thief to appraise an item.  A
    thief gets so good at this skill, he can glean much pertinent
    information from a single glance.  A skilled thief can even
    glean information about an object that somebody else has.

#
"SKILL WARCRY"
    Usable by   :  pal 5
    Usage       :  warcry [<mob>]
    Positions   :  mounted, standing, fighting
    Speed       :  Slow
    Mana        :  0

    This skill is a tremendous combat ability of the paladin.  By
    shouting out the battle cry of his or her god, the paladin can
    actually cause an enemy to feel as though they were physically
    struck.  The more powerful the paladin is in relation to the
    target determines how effective the warcry is.  There is even
    a possibility that the warcry will paralyze an opponent if the
    paladin is much more powerful.

#
"SOCIAL LIST"

A social is a command which performs no technical function.
It is a communication aid, to provide shortcuts to common
tasks and expressions.

"SPELL ACID BLAST"
    Castable by :  mage 6, sorcerer 6
    Usage       :  cast 'acid blast' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  Level d6
    Damage Type :  Acid
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell allows a mage to obliterate opponents with a stream of
    acid.  Not only incredibly damaging to flesh, this spell will destroy
    equipment with great ease.


#
"SPELL AID"
    Castable by :  cleric 4
    Usage       :  cast 'aid' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell grants a pair of small boons to the target, giving them a
    bonus to strike an opponent in combat and healing a small amount of
    damage.


#
"SPELL ANIMAL FRIENDSHIP"
    Castable by :  druid 5, ranger 3
    Usage       :  cast 'animal friendship' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Not Self
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  2
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell can make a weak willed animal follow you and accept your
    commands.  The animal must be less powerful than you, and must be
    of neutral alignment.  Evil and good aligned animals are too strong
    willed to be charmed.  This spell can only be successfully cast once
    per day.  Some similar spells are 'charm person', 'charm monster', and
    'charm vegetable'.


#
"SPELL ANIMAL GROWTH"
    Castable by :  druid 35, ranger 35
    Usage       :  cast 'animal growth' <animal mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Not Self
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell can make an animal grow to twice it's natural size,
    but only in naturally occurring animals.  A polymorphed creature
    can not be targeted by this spell.  The creature has to be
    significantly weaker than the caster, stronger creatures shrug
    off the effects of the magic, which grants greater stamina and
    strength.  The animal will obey any 'order' of the caster.


#
"SPELL ANIMAL SUMMON ONE"
    Castable by :  druid 15, ranger 20
    Usage       :  cast 'animal summon one'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell can only be cast outdoors, and will call an animal
    to do the bidding of the caster.  The power and strength of
    the animal is dependent on the level of the caster, and the
    type of animal summoned is random.  This spell can only be
    cast once every two days, and the animal will obey any
    'order' of the caster.


#

    type of animal summoned is random.  This spell can only be

#
"SPELL ANIMATE DEAD"
    Castable by :  mage 16, cleric 8, sorcerer 16, necromancer 5
    Usage       :  cast 'animate dead' <corpse obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell will take a corpse from a newly deceased creature
    and animate it into a undead servant of the caster.  Even a
    pile of dust from a previously slain undead is enough to
    create a zombie, whose own power is dependent on the level
    of the caster.  The zombie will obey any 'order' of the caster.


#
"SPELL ANIMATE ROCK"
    Castable by :  druid 31
    Usage       :  cast 'animate rock' <rock obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in Room
                   Obj in Inventory
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    If a druid stumbles upon a rock during his or her travels,
    they can use this spell to make the rock animate and follow
    the caster.  Bigger rocks make better servants, so boulders
    are preferable to fist-sized stones.  The rock will obey
    any 'order' of the caster.


#
"SPELL ANTI MAGIC SHELL"
    Castable by :  mage 48, sorcerer 48
    Usage       :  cast 'anti magic shell'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  100
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This powerful spell has an extremely short duration, lasting
    only one hour.  But during that time, no magic may pass into
    or out of the shell.  The mage is perfectly protected from
    all magics, even beneficial spells.  It dispels all current
    spells of the caster, and allows no further casting to take
    place by the caster.  However, spell-like abilities of
    magical weapons and items can be used within a shell to
    great effect.  Only true mages can cast this spell, if a
    player has not devoted him or herself to the casting arts
    they can not possibly learn the intricacies of this spell.


#
"SPELL ARMOR"
    Castable by :  mage 5, cleric 2, sorcerer 5
    Usage       :  cast 'armor' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -

    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No

    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This basic spell gives a decent bonus to the Armor Class of
    the target.  Essentially, it reinforces whatever armor is
    worn with rigid magical energy.  The effect lasts approximately
    one full day.


#
"SPELL ASTRAL WALK"
    Castable by :  cleric 30
    Usage       :  cast 'astral walk' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in World
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This powerful clerical magic allows the caster to send any
    creature to the astral plane.  Anybody who is grouped with
    the target is also shifted to the astral plane.  In the
    astral plane, travel throughout the world is possible by
    entering the color pools, but blindly jumping into pools is
    not recommended for the wise adventurer.  Only grouped
    individuals can be sent, if you cast this spell and the
    target does not get shifted to the other plane, check to
    make sure the target is grouped, even if only with him or
    herself.

#
"SPELL BIND AFFINITY"
    Castable by :  necromancer 48
    Usage       :  cast 'bind affinity'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This unique spell creates a special relationship between the caster
    and where the caster is currently standing.  By casting this spell,
    the place where the spell 'binding' transports you to will change.
    Normally the 'binding' spell returns you to the inn where you last
    rented.  After casting this spell, 'binding' will return you to the
    room where you cast this spell last.  So if you cast this spell
    in The Meeting Square of Karsinya, then casting 'binding' will
    transport you to The Meeting Square.  However, if you are not on
    the same plane as your binding spot, the spell 'binding' won't
    be able to transport you to it.


#
"SPELL BINDING"
    Castable by :  necromancer 16
    Usage       :  cast 'binding'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell functions much like the spell 'word of recall' for
    clerics.  It will transport you instantly from wherever you are
    to your binding spot.  Normally, your binding spot is the inn
    where you last rented.  However through the use of 'bind affinity'
    you can change that spot to wherever you desire.  'Binding' will
    only work if you are on the same plane as your current binding spot.


#
"SPELL BLADE BARRIER"
    Castable by :  cleric 45
    Usage       :  cast 'blade barrier'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  8-64
    Damage Type :  Slash
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  40
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell is one of the most devastating defensive spells ever
    crafted.  Any cleric casting this spell is instantly surrounded
    by a glittering shield of whirling blades.  These blades flash
    through the air, cutting any opponent who dares to attack the
    caster.  The only way for an opponent to hit you safely is if
    they also have a 'blade barrier' spell in place, in which case
    the two spells spark and clash, but do no damage to the people
    involved.  It is impossible to have both 'blade barrier' and
    any other defensive shield spell in place, such as 'fireshield'
    or 'chillshield'.

"SPELL BLINDNESS"
    Castable by :  mage 12, cleric 14, sorcerer 12

    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent

    much easier to hit in combat, and making it much harder for

#
"SPELL BURNING HANDS"
    Castable by :  mage 6, sorcerer 6
    Usage       :  cast 'burning hands'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  2-5 + (Level / 2)
    Damage Type :  Fire
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    The most basic magic capable of doing damage to multiple opponents,
    this spell will shoot forth a sheet of flames from the caster's
    hands.  However, if an opponent is quick enough, they will be able
    to avoid the flames altogether, leaving them unharmed.  If this
    spell is cast in a dark room, any creature using infravision to
    see will have a chance of being temporarily blinded by the heat.
    If any of the victims has wings, they have a chance of being burnt
    off by the fire.


#
"SPELL CACAODEMON"
    Castable by :  mage 30, cleric 29, sorcerer 30
    Usage       :  cast 'cacaodemon' <one | two | three | four | five | six>
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A powerful and dangerous summoning spell, this allows the caster to
    tap into the outer planes and summon demons to do his or her bidding.
    There are six demons capable of being summoned by this spell, the
    least powerful summoned by the first spell, and the most powerful
    by the sixth.  A sacrificial offering must be held or wielded by the
    caster, which will likely be destroyed by the summoning.  Summoning
    a demon will tend to lead even the most goodly intentioned people
    down the road towards evil, so be careful when casting this spell,
    it leaves a black stain on your soul.

    Some of the sacrificial items that are known to be of use with this
    spell are:
    a potion brewed by a hag, held by a ghost in the land of Ixzuul
    a whip, a dagger, and a longsword, held in a city protected by a dracolich
    a named dagger, which can be found in the possession of a halfling
    a runed dagger, held by a small man dressed all in yellow in a ruined city


#
"SPELL CALL LIGHTNING"
    Castable by :  cleric 45, druid 18
    Usage       :  cast 'call lightning' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  (Level + 2) d8
    Damage Type :  Electricity
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This powerful spell can destroy opponents harnessing the power of
    nature itself.  Only able to be cast outside, and the weather must
    be at least raining, if not actually storming, it calls bolts of
    lightning down from the heavens to roast the target.  The weather
    can be affected by the spell 'control weather', so that a powerful
    cleric or druid can change a sunny day into a stormy one, and then
    turn the might of the storm on their hapless opponents.
