#
"SPELL CAUSE CRITICAL"
    Castable by :  cleric 10, druid 13
    Usage       :  cast 'cause critical' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  6-27
    Damage Type :  Pure
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  11
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell allows a cleric to cause damage to the target.  There is
    no particular type of damage associated with this spell, it does not
    burn, or cut, or electrocute, but rather causes injuries to appear.
    The cleric must touch his target to cause the damage however, so it
    is possible to waste the spell if the target dodges the cleric's touch.
    It is considered the reverse of the 'cure critical' spell, and has
    sibling spells of 'cause light', 'cause serious', and 'harm'.

"SPELL CHAIN LIGHTNING"

    Difficulty  :  Very Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    his hands that streams from one target to the next.  Each
    target reduces the power of the bolt slightly, and it can not
    reach past eight targets.  By that time the bolt no longer can

#
"SPELL CHANGE FORM"
    Castable by :  druid 12
    Usage       :  cast 'change form' <creature type>
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Only castable twice per day, this spell allows a druid to
    take the form of a desired animal.  The level of the druid
    determines what type of animals are available to change into.
    Once the druid is ready to return to his or her original form,
    they merely type the command 'return'.  In the case that two
    animals are appropriate for the same creature type, (i.e. "bear")
    the spell will default to changing to the more powerful version.

    Level:    Type:         Proper Name:
    ------    -----         ------------
      10      "bear"        Grizzly Bear
      10      "spider"      Bird Spider
      10      "lamia"       Lamia
      10      "lizard"      Snow Lizard
      12      "bear"        Polar Bear
      12      "gator"       Alligator
      13      "basilisk"    Basilisk
      15      "snake"       Giant Snake
      15      "spider"      Huge Poisonous Spider
      16      "lizard"      Giant Lizard
      18      "allosaurus"  Allosaurus
      28      "tiger"       White Bengal Tiger
      30      "mulichort"   Mulichort
      35      "tiger"       Saber-Tooth Tiger
      35      "lion"        Nemean Lion
      35      "salamander"  Salamander


#
"SPELL CHANGESTAFF"
    Castable by :  druid 30
    Usage       :  cast 'changestaff'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This powerful spell enables a druid to change a staff that
    holds magical charges into a powerful mobile tree
    servant.  The druid must be holding the magical staff in
    his hand when the spell is cast.  The tree's loyalty to
    the druid is dependent on the amount of magical charges
    that remained in the staff.  The staff is destroyed in the
    casting of this spell, but the greater the staff's power,
    the longer the tree will remain loyal.  The tree will obey
    every 'order' of the caster.


#
"SPELL CHARM MONSTER"
    Castable by :  mage 10, druid 12, sorcerer 10
    Usage       :  cast 'charm monster' <monster mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell will charm a monster into following the caster.
    The target can not be of any of the player races, such as
    human, elf, dwarf, etc.  It also can not be vegetable in
    nature, such as myconoid, or a treant.  If successful,
    the target will become a loyal servant to the caster,
    following him for an amount of time determined by the
    caster's charisma.  Using the 'order' command allows the
    caster to make his followers do whatever he wishes.  A
    monster that is more powerful than the caster might be
    immune to the spell.  Siblings of this spell are 'charm
    person' and 'charm vegetable' and 'animal friendship'.


#
"SPELL CHARM PERSON"
    Castable by :  mage 4, sorcerer 4
    Usage       :  cast 'charm person' <person mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Not Self
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell enables the caster to charm any member of the
    normal races of the realms, such as human, elf, dwarf, etc.
    It can not target monsters, vegetable creatures, nor
    animals.  If successful, the target will obey every 'order'
    of the caster.  Siblings of this spell are 'charm monster',
    'charm vegetable' and 'animal friendship'.  The person will
    obey any 'order' given by the caster for a period of time
    determined by the charisma of the caster.

"SPELL CHARM VEGETABLE"

    Usage       :  cast 'charm vegetable' <vegetable mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -

    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy

    This allows a druid to convince any animated vegetable, tree,

    every 'order'.  It can not be used to target any type of
    monster, person or animal.  The caster will be followed for

#
"SPELL CHILL TOUCH"
    Castable by :  mage 4, sorcerer 4
    Usage       :  cast 'chill touch' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  Between Level and Level *3
    Damage Type :  Cold
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell infuses the target with a bone deep chill, causing
    great harm.  The damage done by this is strictly dependent on
    the level of the caster.  A 20th level caster will do between
    20 and 60 damage.  If the target manages to dodge the worst
    of the effects of the spell, they will take only half the
    damage from the deadly chill.  If they fail to avoid the spell,
    it will also weaken the target until they warm up.  Being the
    target of multiple castings of this spell will result in dangerous
    levels of weakness.


#
"SPELL CHILLSHIELD"
    Castable by :  necromancer 45
    Usage       :  cast 'chillshield'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  1-6 + (Level / 2)
    Damage Type :  Cold
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  40
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This is a defensive spell, which creates an aura of intense cold
    around you, in the form of blue flames.  Any creature attacking
    you will take some damage from the shield.  However, if you
    attempt to create a 'chillshield' while surrounded by another
    defensive shield, like 'fireshield' or 'blade barrier' the
    'chillshield' will supplant the old defensive spell.  Having this
    spell around you allows you to safely attack an opponent who also
    is guarded by a 'chillshield'.

"SPELL COLOUR SPRAY"
    Castable by :  mage 14, sorcerer 14
    Usage       :  cast 'colour spray' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  4 * Level
    Damage Type :  Energy

    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Slightly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell is a very colorful and powerful way of dealing damage
    to a single opponent.  Essentially gathering 'mana' and throwing
    it only slightly harnessed at the target, this spell can destroy
    equipment easily.


#
"SPELL COMMAND"
    Castable by :  cleric 1
    Usage       :  cast 'command' <mob> <command>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Paralyzation to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  3
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell has severe limitations, but if the opponent is low
    level and is not especially bright, then the cleric can force
    the target to do any command.  The target knows what happened
    and there is nothing stopping them from attacking the caster.


#
"SPELL COMMUNE"
    Castable by :  druid 20, ranger 20
    Usage       :  cast 'commune'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell gives great knowledge about creatures in a
    particular outdoor area.  Casting this spell will let the
    druid or ranger know exactly what mobs are outdoors in
    the area surrounding the caster.


#
"SPELL COMPREHEND LANGUAGES"
    Castable by :  mage 1, cleric 3, sorcerer 1
    Usage       :  cast 'comprehend languages' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room

    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell grants the target the ability to comprehend any
    spoken language used in the world.  It does not allow the
    target to 'speak' in any language unknown to him or her.


#
"SPELL CONE OF COLD"
    Castable by :  mage 17, sorcerer 17
    Usage       :  cast 'cone of cold'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  Level d5
    Damage Type :  Cold
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Slightly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    The caster shoots a cone of blistering cold from his palm when
    this spell is cast.  Starting at a single point in his hand,
    the cold spreads out rapidly, able to target all creatures
    who are not part of the caster's group.


#
"SPELL CONJURE ELEMENTAL"
    Castable by :  mage 16, cleric 13, druid 11, sorcerer 16
    Usage       :  cast 'conjure elemental' <fire | earth | water | air>
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell enables the summoning of a powerful elemental to
    follow and aid the caster.  There is a material component
    to this spell, which determines what type of elemental is
    summoned by this spell.  The material components are some
    magical stones that are usually found in the possession of
    lamias.  As might be expected, the stones are somewhat
    logical components for the different elemental types.
    A fiery red stone, a dull stone, a pale blue stone, and a
    clear stone are commonly known stones that work for
    this spell.  Any elemental summoned by this spell will remain
    loyal for almost a full day.


#
"SPELL CONTINUAL LIGHT"
    Castable by :  mage 10, cleric 26, druid 16, sorcerer 10
    Usage       :  cast 'continual light'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This more advanced version of the 'light' spell creates
    a magical light source.  A glowing ball of mana-powered
    light appears, and can be used by anybody to light the
    area around them.  The light source from this spell lasts
    forever.


#
"SPELL CONTROL WEATHER"
    Castable by :  cleric 26, druid 15
    Usage       :  cast 'control weather' <better | worse>
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  25
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    By using this spell, the caster can alter the very powerful
    forces of nature.  Making vast alterations in the weather
    patterns of the world is possible.  By indicating whether
    the caster wishes the weather to become 'better' or 'worse',
    the caster can shift the weather one step at a time.  Through
    multiple castings of this spell, the cleric or druid could
    make a cloudless day into a stormy one, or a blizzard into a
    sunny day.  This spell is often used to worsen the weather to
    generate a storm so that the spell 'call lightning' can be
    used.


#
"SPELL CREATE FOOD"
    Castable by :  cleric 5
    Usage       :  cast 'create food'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell will create a nourishing mushroom to eat.  While
    not particularly appetizing, it is very filling.  The mushroom
    appears on the ground in front of the caster.  Any person can
    pick it up and eat it.


#
"SPELL CREATE WATER"
    Castable by :  cleric 2
    Usage       :  cast 'create water' <liquid container obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in Inventory
                   Obj Equipped
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    If the cleric has a liquid container available, like a cup or
    a barrel, this spell will fill it with water.  The amount of
    the water created is dependent on the level of the caster and
    the weather conditions.  It is far easier to fill a cup with
    water if it is raining out than if it is sunny.  This spell
    does not create a drink container.


#
"SPELL CREEPING DEATH"
    Castable by :  druid 45
    Usage       :  cast 'creeping death' <north | east | south |
                                          west | up | down>
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  600-1000
    Damage Type :  Pure
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This extremely powerful, special magic can result in devastating
    damage and great danger to all.  Casting this spell creates an
    almost completely uncontrolled swarm of devouring insects.
    Whatever gets in their way is killed until the swarm has
    dissipated or is destroyed.  Casting this spell is so draining
    that the druid collapses immediately after for a short period
    of time.  His or her last conscious thought pushes the swarm
    in a desired direction.  Once there, the swarm will kill
    indiscriminately, and even has a chance to wander around into
    other areas once it has devoured all in that room. It might even
    wander back into the room with the caster, which could be deadly
    for it's own creator.


#
"SPELL CURE BLIND"
    Castable by :  cleric 6
    Usage       :  cast 'cure blind' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell will alleviate any blindness inflicted on any
    creature.  Once complete, the target's sight is restored
    instantly.  This includes blindness caused by 'clinging
    darkness', 'blindness', 'power word blind', 'psionic blast',
    or even special creature abilities.


#
"SPELL CURE CRITIC"
    Castable by :  cleric 10, druid 13
    Usage       :  cast 'cure critic' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  6-27
    Damage Type :  Heal
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  11
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This curative spell is the most powerful short of the spell
    'heal'.  Using it, wounds instantly mend and bruises fade.
    The amount of damage restored by the cleric or druid is
    between 6 and 27 hitpoints.  Sibling spells to this are:
    'cure light', 'cure serious', and 'heal'.

#
"SPELL CURE LIGHT"
    Castable by :  cleric 1, druid 2, paladin 9
    Usage       :  cast 'cure light' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  1-8
    Damage Type :  Heal
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This curative spell is the least powerful of the common
    healing spells available.  Using it, wounds instantly mend
    and bruises fade.  The amount of damage restored by the caster
    is between 1 and 8 hitpoints.  Sibling spells to this are:
    'cure serious', 'cure critic', and 'heal'.


#
"SPELL CURE SERIOUS"
    Castable by :  cleric 7, druid 8, sorcerer 45, paladin 45
    Usage       :  cast 'cure serious' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room

    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes

    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This curative spell is the second least powerful of the common
    healing spells available.  Using it, wounds instantly mend
    and bruises fade.  The amount of damage restored by the caster
    is between 4 and 18 hitpoints.  Sibling spells to this are:
    'cure light', 'cure critic', and 'heal'.


#
"SPELL CURSE"
    Castable by :  mage 13, cleric 12, sorcerer 13
    Usage       :  cast 'curse' <mob | obj>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Obj in Room
                   Obj in Inventory
                   Obj Equipped
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell functions quite the opposite of the spell 'bless'.
    Casting it on a target means that the target will suffer from
    a decreased chance of hitting opponents in battle, and is more
    susceptible to spells involving paralyzation.  The effect lasts
    a long time, in the range of a full week.  However, far more
    insidious is casting this spell on an object.  A cursed object
    becomes unable to be wielded by good aligned creatures, and
    no creature can get rid of it without casting 'remove curse'
    on the item.  If it is a weapon, it also makes the weapon
    less likely to hit in combat.

#
"SPELL DARK EMPATHY"
    Castable by :  necromancer 24
    Usage       :  cast 'dark empathy' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Not Self
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Oddly enough, the necromancer has the capability to heal others
    by transferring his or her own health to the target.  However,
    the life force transfer can not take place between a necromancer
    and a good aligned target, the energies are too different.
    Also, if the necromancer is badly hurt, he or she can not cast
    this spell successfully.  There is an upper limit to the amount
    of damage this will heal similar in power to the 'heal' spell.


#
"SPELL DARK PACT"
    Castable by :  necromancer 36
    Usage       :  cast 'dark pact'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  33
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    For a handful of hours, this spell creates a contract with the
    dark powers of the world.  Essentially trading life force for
    magical power, this spell reduces your ability to regain your
    health in exchange for a larger mana regeneration amount.  The
    magical power spent on this spell is almost completely offset
    within the first hour of the pact.


#
"SPELL DARKTRAVEL"
    Castable by :  necromancer 39
    Usage       :  cast 'darktravel' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in World
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Using this spell, the necromancer is able to walk through the
    darkness of the shadow realms to appear in the presence of the
    target.  However, this spell has some limitations.  If the target
    is not on the normal plane, the shadow realm has no access to them.
    Obviously this means that if you are on a different plane than your
    home plane, you also have no access to the shadow realm.  Also there
    are some magical counters to this spell, which prevents magical
    transport of any kind to the target.  A final warning, if your
    concentration falters while you travel the shadow realm, there is no
    telling where you might end up.


#
"SPELL DECAY"
    Castable by :  necromancer 18
    Usage       :  cast 'decay' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  4-20
    Damage Type :  Poison
    Saving Throw:  vs. Paralyzation to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell has a quick short term effect, and then a more
    lasting debilitating effect.  By casting this spell, the
    necromancer uses his touch to begin a necrotic illness
    in the target.  Immediately the target's internal organs
    spasm, causing damage, but more insidiously, for almost
    a handful of hours, the decay continues, eating away at
    the body of the target.  Forget about healing or regaining
    mana while under the effect of this spell, and also most
    races take massive damage every hour from this spell, as
    the spell literally liquifies the insides of the target.
    Halflings are somewhat resistant to this spell, taking
    less damage than other races.


#
"SPELL DETECT EVIL"
    Castable by :  cleric 1, druid 6
    Usage       :  cast 'detect evil' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell will help the target to identify who is currently
    on the path of selfishness and darkness.  The taint of evil
    will show itself as a red aura surrounding any evil creature.
    It also will give a red glow to an object if the item is
    not usable by a good creature.  The spell can last a very long
    time if cast by a high level caster.


#
"SPELL DETECT GOOD"
    Castable by :  cleric 1, druid 6
    Usage       :  cast 'detect good' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell will help the target to identify who is currently
    on the path of righteousness and light.  The aura of goodness
    will show itself as a white aura surrounding any good creature.
    It also will give a white glow to an object if the item is
    not usable by an evil creature.  The spell can last a very long
    time if cast by a high level caster.


#
"SPELL DETECT INVISIBILITY"
    Castable by :  mage 2, cleric 5, druid 7, sorcerer 2, bard 6, necromancer 8
    Usage       :  cast 'detect invisibility' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    A staple of most magic users, this spell will allow the
    target to see people and items that have been rendered invisible
    by magic.  It does not do anything to help reveal creatures who
    are hidden from normal view.  The spell can last a very long time,
    depending on the level of the caster.


#
"SPELL DETECT MAGIC"
    Castable by :  mage 1, cleric 3, druid 5, sorcerer 1, bard 5, necromancer 3
    Usage       :  cast 'detect magic' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    A commonly used spell, castable by most magic users, this spell
    shows the target a blue glow surrounding items that carry a
    magical enchantment.  The spell lasts a long time, especially when
    cast by a high level magic user.


#
"SPELL DETECT POISON"
    Castable by :  druid 1, ranger 3
    Usage       :  cast 'detect poison' <mob | food obj | drink container obj>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Obj in Inventory
                   Obj Equipped
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    Using this spell reveals all sorts of poisoning to the caster.
    If the target is a creature, then you will sense if poison
    burns in their blood.  If the target is an food object, it will
    tell you whether the food is poisoned.  The spell also works on
    drink containers, so if you have stumbled across a suspicious
    cup of liquid, this spell may save you from the wracking pains
    of being poisoned.


#
"SPELL DISEASE"
    Castable by :  necromancer 1
    Usage       :  cast 'disease' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  1-8
    Damage Type :  Poison
    Saving Throw:  vs. Paralyzation to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell allows the necromancer to touch the target and
    instantly make them magically suffer the final stages of
    the plague.  Instantly, the target takes damage as his or
    her body is wracked by chills and sores appear.  Then
    over the course of the next half day, the disease ravages
    the body, eventually running it's course.  Halflings are
    naturally resistant to the spell, taking less damage than
    other races.


#
"SPELL DISINTEGRATE"
    Castable by :  mage 48, sorcerer 48
    Usage       :  cast 'disintegrate' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  Level d10
    Damage Type :  Energy
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  45
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Fairly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    One of the most devastating spells ever created, this magic
    has been the death and salvation of many adventurers.  The
    spell basically attempts to scatter the target into many
    tiny little pieces.  If an opponent is tough enough, they
    might last through the effect, otherwise they cease to exist.
    This spell is incredibly destructive to equipment, if you
    are hit by a couple of these spells and still survive, you
    will likely have little equipment left in one piece.  Most
    equipment doesn't even become ruined scraps, but rather
    disappears in a puff of smoke.


#
"SPELL DISPEL EVIL"
    Castable by :  cleric 20
    Usage       :  cast 'dispel evil' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    The bane of other dimension creatures, this spell will send
    them back screaming into their home plane.  While not
    technically killing the creature, it does defeat them for
    a period of time.  If the creature resists the spell, they
    will take some damage, but will continue to exist in this
    plane.  This spell works against evil creatures, and is
    generally used by good aligned clerics.  Evil clerics can
    cast it, but it is at their own peril.


#
"SPELL DISPEL GOOD"
    Castable by :  cleric 20
    Usage       :  cast 'dispel good' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    The bane of other dimension creatures, this spell will send
    them back screaming into their home plane.  While not
    technically killing the creature, it does defeat them for
    a period of time.  If the creature resists the spell, they
    will take some damage, but will continue to exist in this
    plane.  This spell works against good creatures, and is
    generally used by evil aligned clerics.  Good clerics can
    cast it, but it is at their own peril.


#
"SPELL DISPEL MAGIC"
    Castable by :  mage 9, cleric 10, druid 9, sorcerer 9, necromancer 14
    Usage       :  cast 'dispel magic' [<mob | obj>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Obj in Room
                   Obj in Inventory
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate (Special, see below)
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    A basic spell and one of the most important spells a magic user can
    learn.  This spell removes magical effects from the target.  If
    the target is affected by the 'sanctuary' spell, casting 'dispel
    magic' can remove it from them.  Think of this spell as a contest
    between the caster and the magic user who cast the spells the
    'dispel magic' wants to dispel.  'Dispel magic' will attempt to
    remove each magical effect on the target.  If the caster is the
    equal or more powerful than the magic, then the magic is dispelled.
    If the caster is less powerful than the magic, then the creature that
    has the magical effect can resist the attempt to remove it.  So a less
    powerful caster could potentially dispel only some of the magical
    effects of a target.  Only very powerful magic users can dispel the
    magical effects of items, but once that has been done, it allows
    the spell 'enchant weapon' or 'enchant armor' to be cast.


#
"SPELL DOMINATE UNDEAD"
    Castable by :  necromancer 6
    Usage       :  cast 'dominate undead' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Paralyzation to Negate
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Using this spell, the caster can command allegiance from any
    undead creature, provided that creature isn't much more
    powerful than the caster.  The undead will follow the
    caster for a period of time determined by how charismatic
    the caster is.


#
"SPELL DRAGON BREATH"
    Castable by :
    Usage       :  cast 'dragon breath'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  -

"SPELL EARTHQUAKE"
    Castable by :  cleric 15
    Usage       :  cast 'earthquake'

    Damage      :  2-5 + Level
    Damage Type :  Pure
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This unusual spell is one of the few purely offensive
    weapons in the cleric's arsenal.  Flying creatures are
    immune to the damage caused by this spell, but weak
    creatures are likely to be swallowed up by the very
    ground.  Any allies of the caster are safe from harm,
    but the effects of this spell can be felt from very
    far away.

"SPELL ENCHANT ARMOR"
    Castable by :  mage 16, sorcerer 16, necromancer 17
    Usage       :  cast 'enchant armor' <armor obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in Inventory
                   Obj Equipped
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  100
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell allows the caster to grant magical enhancements to
    non-magical armor.  There are some restrictions to this,
    especially if the armor has some similar magical effects to the
    ones granted by this spell.  Once the spell has been cast,
    the armor will receive some improvement to it's protective
    qualities.  The amount of the improvement is based on the power
    of the caster.  After the spell has been cast, the armor will
    be magical, and it's aura will be identical to the aura of the
    caster.


#
"SPELL ENCHANT WEAPON"
    Castable by :  mage 14, sorcerer 14, necromancer 21
    Usage       :  cast 'enchant weapon' <weapon obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in Inventory
                   Obj Equipped
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  100
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell allows the caster to give magical enhancements to
    non-magical weapons.  As long as the weapon does not already
    have similar magic-like effects to those granted by this spell,
    it can be made to hit more often and harder in combat.  Higher
    level casters grant more powerful bonuses.  The weapon will
    be magical if this spell is successful, and it's aura will
    match the aura of the caster.


#
"SPELL ENDURE COLD"
    Castable by :  necromancer 12
    Usage       :  cast 'endure cold'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  25
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    By casting this spell, the necromancer brings some of the chill
    of the shadow realm into his or her body.  By doing so, the
    body can withstand great extremes of exterior coldness.  This
    resistance to cold will mean that any cold-based attack will do
    only 1/2 the damage as it would normally.  The amount of time
    the caster can hold the unnatural chill is dependent on the level
    of the caster, from only a pair of hours to almost half of a day.


#
"SPELL ENERGY DRAIN"
    Castable by :  mage 22, sorcerer 22, necromancer 15
    Usage       :  cast 'energy drain' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  35
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Fairly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This evil magical act will cause the target's life force to be
    permanently diminished.  Casting this spell is considered an
    evil act, and will tend to make the caster evil.  If the victim
    does not save, the caster will strip them of a level, and all
    the abilities and stats that go along with that level.  If a
    15th level cleric is struck by this spell, he or she will now
    be 14th level and will lose access to spells, such as 'earthquake'.
    Every vital statistic will drop accordingly.  The only way to get
    back the lost life force is to have a cleric cast 'energy restore'
    on you soon.  This spell has a chance of backfiring on the caster,
    so be careful using it.

#
"SPELL ENERGY RESTORE"
    Castable by :  cleric 48
    Usage       :  cast 'energy restore' <player>
    Targets     :  Player in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    An incredibly useful spell, this is the cleric's response to the
    life draining abilities of undead and evil mages.  If the target
    has been recently drained, this spell will return that life force
    in full to them.  However, in doing so, the caster will end up
    exhausted and unable to move for a significant period of time.


#

    This spell grants the paladin a temporary boost to his or her

    among them, practicing new spells becomes easier, and mana is
    recovered more swiftly.

"SPELL ENTANGLE"
    Castable by :  druid 16
    Usage       :  cast 'entangle' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent

    Casting Time:  Fast

    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell is very powerful, but also very limited in scope.
    It can only be cast outdoors in a forest, but if it is
    successfully cast, the hands of nature will reach out and
    grasp the victim.  All the plants nearby will wrap the victim
    up so tightly that they can not move a muscle, and in fact
    are considered paralyzed for a short period of time.


#
"SPELL EYE OF THE DEAD"
    Castable by :  necromancer 26
    Usage       :  cast 'eye of the dead'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  25
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell grants the necromancer the ability to see everything
    around him or her.  Essentially, the spirits of the dead take
    up residence in one of the eyes of the caster.  Since the dead
    spirits have perceptions far different from our own, this spell
    gives the necromancer the equivalent of the cleric spell 'true
    sight'.  It lasts almost for a full day, before the spirits
    clamber for their release.

"SPELL FAERIE FIRE"
    Castable by :  mage 5, cleric 4, druid 1, sorcerer 5, ranger 7

                   Not Self

    in a pink light.  However, that pink light serves to make the

#
"SPELL FAERIE FOG"
    Castable by :  mage 16, cleric 11, druid 10, sorcerer 16
    Usage       :  cast 'faerie fog'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  Special
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell creates a billowing cloud of purple smoke, which
    fills the area quickly and completely.  The cloud is not
    completely opaque and it has the tendency to clearly outline
    shapes, which means that you can see the edges of invisible
    creatures, and will even make hidden creatures visible.  If
    the hidden creature resists the spell, they are able to
    re-hide themselves after being revealed.  It will not reveal
    any allies of the caster, so the invisible compatriots of the
    caster are safe from detection.

#
"SPELL FEEBLEMIND"
    Castable by :  mage 34, sorcerer 34
    Usage       :  cast 'feeblemind' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Slightly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    The bane of spell casters and psionists everywhere, this spell
    is a death sentence for anybody who relies on spells to stay
    alive.  If the victim fails to shake off the effect, they
    literally become almost moronic.  The level of intelligence
    drops like a rock, and the ability to cast spells successfully
    plummets.  Most psionist abilities are impossible to attempt
    while under the influence of this spell, and forget about magic
    spells.  Psionists have a defense against the spell using
    'mindblank', otherwise a victim can expect to be in this state
    for a full day.

    This spell gives the caster the ability to see traps before
    they are sprung.  It only tends to work on mechanical traps,

    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell is the epitome of the necromancer's art.  It basically

    otherworldly minions.  If the target is very unlucky, then the
    soul is instantly ripped free.  Otherwise the struggle to keep the

"SPELL FIREBALL"
    Castable by :  mage 25, sorcerer 25
    Usage       :  cast 'fireball'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  Level d8
    Damage Type :  Fire
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  40
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Slightly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Possibly the most well known spell in the world, this
    standard part of the magic user's repertoire is deadly
    and powerful.  Starting out as a pea-sized pebble of
    fire streaking from the caster's finger, it expands
    and when reaching the optimum distance, explodes,
    scorching any creature who is not allied with the caster.
    If the room is dark, any victims who are using infravision
    to see could be blinded, and it could burn the wings of
    any flying race.


#
"SPELL FIRESHIELD"
    Castable by :  mage 40, druid 48, sorcerer 40
    Usage       :  cast 'fireshield'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  1-6 + (Level / 2)
    Damage Type :  Fire
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  40
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This is a defensive spell, which creates an aura of intense heat
    around you, in the form of red flames.  Any creature attacking
    you will take some damage from the shield.  However, if you
    attempt to create a 'fireshield' while surrounded by another
    defensive shield, like 'chillshield' or 'blade barrier' the
    'fireshield' will supplant the old defensive spell.  Having this
    spell around you allows you to safely attack an opponent who also
    is guarded by a 'fireshield'.


#
"SPELL FIRESTORM"
    Castable by :  druid 22
    Usage       :  cast 'firestorm'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  3-17 + Level

    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Akin to the mage and sorcerer spell 'fireball', this spell sends
    a whirling mass of flame across a room, burning any creature not
    allied with the caster.  If the spell is cast in a dark room,
    a victim using infravision could be temporarily blinded.  Also
    a winged creature could find themselves unable to fly due to
    burnt wings.

#
"SPELL DARKNESS"
    Castable by :  mage 5, cleric 3, druid 3, sorcerer 5, necromancer 5
    Usage       :  cast 'darkness' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This common spell has a simple effect, to surround the target with
    an opaque globe of darkness.  It best serves to hide the spells that
    might be visible on the target.  For instance, if a creature has the
    spell 'sanctuary' cast on them, 'darkness' would hide the white glow
    that is associated with the 'sanctuary' spell.  Also the races that
    have grown accustomed to living in total darkness can use this spell
    to prevent suffering from the glare of the daylight cast by bright
    light sources.


#
"SPELL GOLEM"
    Castable by :  cleric 15
    Usage       :  cast 'golem'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell allows a cleric to animate a set of armor, creating
    a golem of great strength and loyalty.  To cast this spell the
    cleric must lay out a set of armor on the ground in front of
    him or her.  The pieces of armor that are required for this
    spell are: boots, gloves, jacket, sleeves, leggings, and helm.
    Without all of these parts, they spell will fail.  However, the
    stronger the armor used to fuel the spell, the more powerful the
    golem will be.


#
"SPELL GOODBERRY"
    Castable by :  druid 4, ranger 10
    Usage       :  cast 'goodberry'
    Targets     :  None

    Casting Time:  Fast

    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell can only be cast outdoors, and it provides the caster
    with a berry that both satisfies hunger and will heal the person
    who eats it of a small amount of damage.

"SPELL GUST OF WIND"
    Castable by :  mage 10, sorcerer 10
    Usage       :  cast 'gust of wind'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  2
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Using this spell, the caster can cause a huge gust of wind
    to spring forth suddenly, knocking down the people in the
    area.  Some creatures will be lucky enough to keep standing,
    but those that don't will have to struggle to their feet
    before they can take any more actions.


#
"SPELL HARM"
    Castable by :  cleric 25
    Usage       :  cast 'harm' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  100
    Damage Type :  Pure
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  35
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Nearly Impossible
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    An evil use of the classic healing abilities of clerics,
    this spell is the antithesis of the 'heal' spell.  If the
    caster succeeds in the spell and manages to touch the
    target, it will cause wounds to suddenly appear.  A spell
    of this magnitude can cause grievous injuries, external
    and internal, and can mean a major swing in a battle.
    Siblings of this spell are 'cause light', 'cause serious',
    and 'cause critical'.


#
"SPELL HASTE"
    Castable by :  mage 23, sorcerer 23
    Usage       :  cast 'haste' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    A spell that has a trade-off of benefits and consequences.
    The benefit of this spell is that for a period of time based
    on the power of the caster, the target moves almost twice as
    quickly as normal.  Most noticeable in combat, the target
    will attack more often than usual.  Casting this spell will
    also remove the effects of the 'slow' spell.  The major
    consequence to this spell is that the target is aged a full
    year at the time the spell is cast.  Even if the spell is
    dispelled after only an hour, the target is still going to
    be a year older than they were before the spell was cast.
    Eventually, aging will affect creatures, making them slower,
    weaker, and decrepit.


#
"SPELL HEAL"
    Castable by :  cleric 25
    Usage       :  cast 'heal' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Incredibly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    The primary calling of the cleric is to heal, and this spell
    represents that for anybody who worships the gods.  It will
    heal up to 100 points of damage, but it can not heal the
    target to full health, it will always be a little short.
    The gods decree this as a reminder of their power and the
    cost of their healing.  The opposite of this spell is 'harm'
    and the siblings are, 'cure light', 'cure serious', 'cure
    critical'.


#
"SPELL HEAT STUFF"
    Castable by :  druid 23
    Usage       :  cast 'heat stuff' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  Special
    Damage Type :  Fire
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Casting this spell results great woe for those targets who
    wear metal armor and wield metal weapons.  If the druid
    successfully touches the victim, the metal objects of that
    creature begin to heat up, eventually becoming hot enough
    to scorch flesh badly.  Not only that, but the heating
    of the metal also causes the victim's dexterity to suffer
    because of the constant attempts to avoid the hot equipment.
    The amount of damage caused by this spell is dependent on
    how much metal the victim is wearing.  If the victim manages
    to remove all metal equipment quickly, they will suffer no
    damage.  Otherwise the victim will take up to 2 point of
    damage per metal item worn.


#
"SPELL HEROES FEAST"
    Castable by :  cleric 24
    Usage       :  cast 'heroes feast'
    Targets     :  All in Group
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  40
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    A great investment spell, casting this has many effects.
    First off, it completely refreshes the allies of the caster,
    similar to the 'refresh' or 'second wind' spell.  The second
    effect is to satiate the members of the group, making them
    feel as though they've eaten a wonderful meal and drank the
    purest of waters.


#
"SPELL HOLY ARMOR"

    Saving Throw:  -

    Scribe/Brew :  No

    own armor with magical force.  The effect lasts for a full

    'armor'.

"SPELL HOLY STRENGTH"

    Targets     :  Self Only

    a period of time determined by the power of the paladin
    invoking the ritual, the paladin will wield great strength,
    which could make them even more deadly when facing their
    evil foes.


#
"SPELL HOLY WORD"
    Castable by :
    Usage       :  cast 'holy word'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  Special
    Damage Type :  Pure
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Immensely Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A powerful word, filled with the holy might of the gods can
    render weaker creatures helpless, or even dead.  Depending
    on the power of the victims, they will either be struck dead,
    paralyzed, blinded, or stunned for a short time.  However,
    if they are too powerful, they will not be effected at all.
    This is the spell to use against evil creatures, unlike it's
    twin, 'unholy word', which is used against good creatures.


#
"SPELL ICE STORM"
    Castable by :  mage 11, sorcerer 11
    Usage       :  cast 'ice storm'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  Level d4
    Damage Type :  Cold
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Casting this spell creates a brief, localized ice storm to
    appear in the immediate area of the caster.  Any person
    not allied with the caster is pounded by hail and cut by
    sleet.  It lasts only briefly, which is fortunate for it's
    victims.


#
"SPELL IDENTIFY"
    Castable by :  mage 10, cleric 16, sorcerer 10
    Usage       :  cast 'identify' <mob> | <obj>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Obj in Room
                   Obj in Inventory
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell is a great boon to gathering knowledge of this world.
    Casting it on an object imparts almost perfect knowledge about
    that object.  Only the most secret of details remains hidden from
    the spell.  It can also be used on individuals, but only of the
    adventuring type.  Casting it on a fellow adventurer grants a great
    deal of knowledge about that person, provided the magic user is
    powerful enough.  However, for a monster the magic is not strong
    enough, the 'know monster' spell is needed.


#
"SPELL INCENDIARY CLOUD"
    Castable by :  mage 45, sorcerer 45
    Usage       :  cast 'incendiary cloud'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  Level d10
    Damage Type :  Fire
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  60
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Immensely Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This powerful spell is the most devastating area effect spell
    known to the world.  Essentially, the caster fills the room
    with an extremely flammable gas, which is released from the
    hands.  Once that process is complete, which takes only a
    moment, he lights a spark, turning the whole area into an
    inferno of indescribable torment.  During that time, if the
    room was dark and a creature was using infravision, they may
    be temporarily blinded.  Also this can burn the wings off of
    flying creatures, leaving them grounded.  The fire burns out
    in a moment, leaving behind only the twisted remains of the
    dead, and the incredibly painful injuries of the living.


#
"SPELL INFRAVISION"
    Castable by :  mage 8, druid 5, sorcerer 8
    Usage       :  cast 'infravision' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  7
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell, which powerful casters can make last over a week,
    grants the target infravision.  Infravision can make it possible
    to see in the dark without a light source by allowing the target
    to see into the infrared spectrum.  Heat, not light, becomes the
    patterns of the world around him or her.  However, it does not
    help to describe what the room looks like, nor what objects lie
    on the ground, just the creatures who are in the room with you.


#
"SPELL INSECT GROWTH"
    Castable by :  druid 33
    Usage       :  cast 'insect growth' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Not Self
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell, which can only be cast outdoors on insects, gives
    those insects a powerful boost.  Basically, it doubles the
    insects in size, making them correspondingly more powerful
    in attacking, more resistant to damage, and less likely to be
    affected by spells.  It lasts a full half day, after which
    time the insect regains it's normal size.  This spell does
    nothing to make the insect follow you, and it can not affect
    insects that are too powerful already.  It is best used on
    insects that are roughly half as powerful as the caster.


#
"SPELL INVIS TO ANIMALS"
    Castable by :  druid 11, ranger 8
    Usage       :  cast 'invis to animals'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell is only available to the nature-oriented casters
    of druids and rangers.  For a full day following this spell
    the caster is invisible to all animals, which tends to be
    unintelligent animals such as: predatory animals, fish, birds,
    herbivorous animals, reptiles, kangaroos, insects, and arachnids.
    Once the caster attacks any creature, the invisibility is broken.

#
"SPELL INVIS TO UNDEAD"
    Castable by :  necromancer 2
    Usage       :  cast 'invis to undead'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell is only available to the death-oriented caster
    of necromancy.  For a full day following this spell
    the caster is invisible to all undead.  Useful for not
    attracting attention in graveyards.  Once the caster attacks
    any creature, the invisibility is broken.


#
"SPELL INVISIBILITY"
    Castable by :  mage 4, sorcerer 4
    Usage       :  cast 'invisibility' <mob> | <obj>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Obj in Room
                   Obj in Inventory
                   Obj Equipped
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    The classic spell of invisibility makes the caster impossible
    to see without magical intervention.  While the target can still
    be heard, and he or she can take actions that obviously indicate
    their presence, they can not be seen themselves.  The spell can
    also be cast on objects, making them permanently invisible.  If
    it is cast on a person it lasts a maximum of a day, but is
    dispelled if the caster takes offensive actions against another
    creature.  While invisible, the caster is much harder to hit
    in combat, but combat will likely dispel the invisibility, so it
    is only a momentary advantage.


#
"SPELL IRON SKINS"
    Castable by :  druid 20
    Usage       :  cast 'iron skins'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  65
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Similar in effect to the spell 'mana shield', this magic grants
    the druid a powerful level of protection.  Casting this spell
    makes the earth disgorge some of it's iron bones into forming
    a malleable, many layered skin around the caster.  The number
    and toughness of the skin layers is determined by the power of
    the druid casting the spell.  As each attack occurs, the skins
    start to flake away, until no protection remains.


#
"SPELL KNOCK"
    Castable by :  mage 3, sorcerer 3
    Usage       :  cast 'knock' <doorname> [<north | east | south |
                                             west | up | down>]
    Targets     :  Door
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell gives the mage the ability to open locked doors.
    Thieves can do similarly with their non-magical skills, but
    this spell can not affect anything besides a door, where
    the thief can 'pick' the lock of containers as well.  Casting
    this spell requires that the mage know the name of the door
    he or she wants to affect, which may be just "door" or may
    be a more specific name.  If there are multiple doors of the
    same name, the direction (north, east, south, west, up, down)
    can help to identify the right one.
    example: cast 'knock' door south


#
"SPELL KNOW ALIGNMENT"
    Castable by :  mage 7, cleric 4, druid 2, sorcerer 7, paladin 5
    Usage       :  cast 'know alignment' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    Casting this spell gives you a general idea of how righteous
    and good-hearted a creature is.  If you lack the ability
    to 'detect good' and 'detect evil', this spell will give you
    information you need to not kill something against your own
    character.  It also provides a little better idea of how evil
    or how good a creature is, rather than the white and red
    auras shown by 'detect good' and 'detect evil'.


#
"SPELL KNOW MONSTER"
    Castable by :  mage 9, sorcerer 9
    Usage       :  cast 'know monster' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Not Self
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell is very useful, especially as the power of the caster
    increases.  At low levels, the spell describes only the basics
    of what the target is and how they behave.  At high levels the
    information is very specific and can mean the difference between
    winning and losing a battle.  Information such as race,
    vulnerabilities, immunities, damage, and hit points all become
    available at the higher levels of power.


#
"SPELL LIFE DRAW"
    Castable by :  necromancer 15
    Usage       :  cast 'life draw' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  ((Level / 10) + 3) d6 +3
    Damage Type :  Drain
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  12
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    If the target of this spell does not have any life force,
    like most undead, then it is not effective.  If the target
    does have life force, then the necromancer can do something
    that is repugnant to most people.  He or she can suck the
    life force from another being and transfer it to him or
    herself.  If the target has resistance to draining magic
    or is protected by the spell 'sanctuary', then the amount
    of life stolen is reduced.  For an hour, the necromancer
    can actually steal more life force than he can hold
    naturally, but after an hour, the life force drains away.
    The siblings of this spell are 'life leech', 'life tap',
    and 'soul steal'.

#
"SPELL LIGHT"
    Castable by :  mage 1, cleric 2, druid 3, sorcerer 1
    Usage       :  cast 'light'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell creates a magical light source.  A glowing ball
    of mana-powered light appears, and can be used by anybody
    to light the area around them.  The light source from this
    spell lasts at least a day, and as much as three days if
    cast by a high level magic user.  A sibling of this spell
    is the 'continual light' spell.


#
"SPELL LIGHTNING BOLT"
    Castable by :  mage 10, sorcerer 10
    Usage       :  cast 'lightning bolt' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  Level d6
    Damage Type :  Electricity
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A classic of the tales of magic throwing wizards, by pointing
    at a target, this spell will release a bolt of lightning that
    streaks towards the target.  If the victim is lucky, it will
    only graze him or her, nevertheless it will be a very painful
    experience.


#
"SPELL LOCATE OBJECT"
    Castable by :  cleric 11
    Usage       :  cast 'locate object' <obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in World
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A very useful spell, it allows the clerics to tap into the
    gods' omniscience briefly, in a limited fashion.  By
    casting this spell, the cleric will receive an idea of
    where any items whose names match their search criteria.
    However, the spell can't find an object if the realm where
    the object exists hasn't been called into being (see
    'term init').  The cleric only receives partial information
    about the whereabouts of the item, but it should be enough
    to whet the appetite of any treasure hunter.


#
"SPELL MAGIC MISSILE"
    Castable by :  mage 1, sorcerer 1
    Usage       :  cast 'magic missile' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  (((Level / 2) + 1) d4) + (Level / 2) + 1
    Damage Type :  Energy
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    The workhorse of the mage's arsenal, this common spell is a
    good balance between power, cost, and speed.  Although
    simply defeated by the spell 'shield', it otherwise has
    few drawbacks.  A simple transformation of mana into energy,
    it sends darts of magical energy at the target.  The darts
    slam into the target, and the more powerful the caster, the
    more powerful the darts.  A 1st level caster will do 2-5
    points of damage, a 20th level caster will do 22-55 points
    of damage, and a 50th level arch mage will do 52-130 points
    of damage.


#
"SPELL MAJOR INVULNERABILITY"
    Castable by :  mage 27, sorcerer 27, necromancer 30
    Usage       :  cast 'major invulnerability'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell has a somewhat short duration, lasting only a handful
    of hours, even when cast by the most powerful of mages.  During
    that time, the caster is encased by a globe of magic that makes
    the caster immune to spells of levels 6-10.  Some sample spells
    this works against are: 'fear', 'lightning bolt', and 'weakness'.
    Sibling spells to this one are: 'minor invulnerability' and
    'anti magic shell'.

#
"SPELL MAJOR TRACK"
    Castable by :  mage 20, druid 17, sorcerer 20
    Usage       :  cast 'major track' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    Using this spell, the caster can give the target the ability
    to guide themselves magically towards a creature.  Using the
    'track' command, the recipient of this spell can be led, step
    by step, towards the target if the target is in range.  The
    path shows up as a faint green trail, following it will
    take you to the target.  The spell lasts a long time, perhaps
    more than four days when cast by a high level magic user.
    A less powerful version of this spell is 'minor track'.


#
"SPELL MANA"
    Castable by :
    Usage       :  cast 'mana'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No

    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This is not a spell meant for mortals, but it regenerates magical
    power in the caster.


#
"SPELL MANA SHIELD"
    Castable by :  mage 14, sorcerer 14
    Usage       :  cast 'mana shield'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A spell with a short duration but potentially life saving effect,
    mana shield is a unique type of armor.  By casting this spell,
    the caster, whose main focus must be as a mage, gains the ability
    to use his magical power as a perfect defense.  While the spell
    lasts, any damage taken by the mage is first absorbed by the
    mana shield, but at the cost of his or her mana supply.  If a mage
    takes 10 points of damage from an attack, his mana shield prevents the
    damage, but the mage's supply of mana is reduced by the same amount
    of 10.  So it is both a benefit and a curse, while it protects the
    caster from harm, it also reduces the ability of the mage to cast
    spells to defeat a foe.  When the mage's mana runs out, so does
    the mana shield.

"SPELL MEND BONES"
    Castable by :  necromancer 10
    Usage       :  cast 'mend bones' [<undead mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  11
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell is only useful against undead targets, and is
    typically used by the necromancer on his own followers.
    Casting this spell acts like a 'cure critical' cast by
    a cleric, healing between 6-27 points of damage, but
    only on undead, other beings can not benefit from it.


#
"SPELL METEOR SWARM"
    Castable by :  mage 36, sorcerer 36
    Usage       :  cast 'meteor swarm' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  Level d12
    Damage Type :  Fire
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  35
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Immensely Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    The most powerful spell ever crafted that targets a single victim,
    this spell is a devastating opening strike.  Basically it calls
    the wrath of the heavens down on the target.  The target pointed
    at by the mage becomes the landing point of magically created
    meteors falling from above at speeds greater than any diving
    falcon.  The meteors are very hot, and cause horrific burns
    to the victim.  If the victim is lucky, they might avoid the
    full force of the swarm.

"SPELL MINOR CREATION"
    Castable by :  mage 8, sorcerer 8
    Usage       :  cast 'minor creation' <sword | shield | bag |
                                          raft | barrel | bread>
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Using his own reserves of magical power, the caster can change
    mana into material items.  The material items able to be crafted
    by this are limited, but can be useful.  The raft can be used to
    float on a lake or river, the barrel comes filled with water, the
    bag can hold items, the bread can be eaten, and the sword and shield,
    although not very powerful, might be better than nothing in a pinch.

"SPELL MIST OF DEATH"
    Castable by :  necromancer 28
    Usage       :  cast 'mist of death'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  Level d7
    Damage Type :  Drain
    Saving Throw:  vs. Petrification for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  35
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Immensely Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    to necromancers.  By releasing his own darkness and making it
    a tangible cloud, the necromancer damages the very souls of
    all non-allied creatures in the room, provided they have
    unprotected souls.  In some rare instances, the cloud of
    darkness can instantly snuff out the soul of a victim, but
    regardless, the victims of this spell never forget this
    devastating spell.

"SPELL MONSUM ONE"
    Castable by :  mage 4, sorcerer 4
    Usage       :  cast 'monsum one'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Casting this spell brings a servant to follow and aid the caster.
    Anything the magic user wants the follower to do, he can use the
    command 'order' to make it happen.  The creature appears out of
    thin air and will follow the caster for a period of time determined
    by the charisma of the summoner.  Clever use of these followers can
    mean the difference between living and dying.  This version of the
    monster summoning spells summons a goblin.  The follower can be
    released by the 'dismiss' command.

"SPELL NUMB THE DEAD"
    Castable by :  necromancer 15

                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -

    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    sure that an undead creature is no longer likely to initiate
    attacks on other creatures.  However, it does take the touch
    of the necromancer to remove the hatred from the undead, so
    he or she must successfully touch the mob.

"SPELL PACIFISM"
    Castable by :  paladin 7
    Usage       :  cast 'pacifism' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -

    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell gives the paladin a chance to touch a mob and to
    remove it's desire to initiate combat with other creatures.
    It will not work on a target that has a great deal of hate
    in it's heart, but it will work on most aggressive creatures.


#
"SPELL PARALYZE"
    Castable by :  mage 20, sorcerer 20
    Usage       :  cast 'paralyze' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Paralyzation to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Incredibly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell, which does no damage but it incredibly deadly,
    can instantly make the target immobile.  If the target fails
    to resist the spell, they are effectively helpless.  Fully
    aware, but unable to take any actions.  Not so much as utter
    a syllable, twitch a finger, shuffle the feet, etc.  During
    this time, any opponents are free to beat the living crap
    out of the victim, with no fear of retribution.  If cast by
    a person, the spell lasts no less than a day, and can last
    easily over two days.  Being resistant to hold magics
    can make this spell less effective, being immune can make
    this spell a waste of time.


#
"SPELL PLANT GATE"
    Castable by :  druid 40
    Usage       :  cast 'plant gate' <tree obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in World
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  60
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A truly unique transportation spell, it allows the druid, and
    any creature allied with the druid to move about the world
    through the access points of specific trees.  By standing in
    the room of one tree, and specifying which tree he or she
    wishes to emerge from, the druid can step into one tree and
    step out of another.  The trees are named rather specifically,
    but it is a secret known only to the druids what they are,
    except the tree in the Market Square of Karsinya, which is
    called Tiberius.
