"SPELL POISON"
    Castable by :  cleric 13, druid 8, necromancer 8
    Usage       :  cast 'poison' [<mob> | <food/drink obj>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Not Self
                   Obj in Inventory
                   Obj Equipped
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  Special
    Damage Type :  Poison
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Fairly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell is used to put a magical poison into the veins of
    an opponent, or to make a piece of food, or a container of
    drink deadly.  Becoming poisoned will sap the strength of
    the victim, and also cause them damage, but it doesn't really
    hurt them except when another hour passes.  The poisoning
    can last a very long time, over four days when cast by an
    adept, and each successful casting of the spell makes it last
    even longer.  The only way to rid yourself of this poisoning
    is through time, the 'remove poison' spell, the 'nullify'
    spell, or a potion.  Halflings are resistant to the damage
    caused by this spell.

"SPELL PORTAL"
    Castable by :  mage 43, sorcerer 43
    Usage       :  cast 'portal' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in World
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A powerful spell, that can save great time and effort,
    the 'portal' spell will create a gate between two
    places.  By carefully releasing a great deal of magical
    energy and focussing solely on the target, the mage can
    create a shimmering doorway, which can be accessed using
    'enter portal'.  The portal must originally target a
    creature, the mana forms a link between the caster and
    the target.  Once that link is established, the magic
    will tie to the location of both parties, but only in
    the direction of the flow of magic power.  This means
    that the portal and the end point are stationary, and
    you can only travel one way, from the caster to the
    target.  There are several ways that the spell can
    fail, such as: if the caster and the target are on
    different planes, the target is in a room that repels
    the magical link, the target itself is too powerful
    to successfully link with, or the gods have denied
    the ability to bend space.  You can 'look portal'
    to determine what location was successfully linked.


#
"SPELL PRISMATIC SPRAY"
    Castable by :  mage 17, sorcerer 17
    Usage       :  cast 'prismatic spray'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  Special
    Damage Type :  Pure
    Saving Throw:  Special
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  40
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell can be very powerful, but is completely random in nature.
    By releasing magical energy, in a barely constrained state, the caster
    can produce many types of effects, which show themselves as beams
    of light.  Each creature not allied with the caster is struck by one
    beam.  The colors of the beams of light and the effects are:

    Red, Orange, Yellow - These will cause damage to the victim, the
    victim may Save vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage.

    Green - This beam will 'poison' the target, but they can Save vs. Poison
    to Negate.

    Blue - This beam will 'paralyze' the target it strikes unless they Save
    vs. Paralyzation to Negate.

    Indigo - This beam will 'feeblemind' the target unless they Save vs.
    Spell to Negate.

    Violet - This beam will cause the target to randomly 'teleport' to some
    other location in the world.  They can Save vs. Spell to Negate.

"SPELL PROTECTION FROM COLD"
    Castable by :  cleric 20, druid 21
    Usage       :  cast 'protection from cold'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  40
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell creates a magical barrier against cold based attacks.
    Any damage taken from an attack is reduced by half by this
    protective screen.  It doesn't last long, even a powerful
    caster will only be protected for a handful of hours.  If the
    caster already is resistant to cold, then this spell does not
    provide any more protection.

    dragons, acid-spitting worms, giant slugs and other similar creatures

"SPELL PROTECTION FROM EVIL"
    Castable by :  cleric 7, paladin 20, ranger 25
    Usage       :  cast 'protection from evil' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell provides some general combat benefits when fighting
    evil creatures.  By forming a weak barrier around the target, it
    gives the target and his or her evil opponents just enough of a
    pause to give the protected person combat bonuses, both to hit
    evil opponents, and to dodge the attacks of evil opponents.  This
    spell lasts a full day.  This spell is the single target variant of
    'protection from evil group' and the opposite of 'protection from
    good'.

    evil opponents, and to dodge the attacks of evil opponents.  This
    spell lasts a full day, and is the exact same as 'protection from
    evil' and the exact opposite of 'protection from good group'.

"SPELL POWER WORD BLIND"
    Castable by :  mage 16, sorcerer 16
    Usage       :  cast 'power word blind' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  Special
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A single word of power, infused with magical energy, can have
    devastating effect on the target.  The difference between this
    and the spell 'blindness' is that the target does not get a chance
    to avoid the effect.  Either they are weak and able to be affected,
    or they are immune to the spell entirely.  Another spell of the
    same type is 'power word kill'.


#
"SPELL POWER WORD KILL"
    Castable by :  mage 23, sorcerer 23
    Usage       :  cast 'power word kill' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  Special
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Slightly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A single word of power, infused with magical energy, can have
    devastating effect on the target.  This spell can instantly snuff
    out the life of the target, shattering their connection between
    their body and soul.  The spell is so devastating that it has severe
    limitations on it's use.  Either they are weak and able to be affected,
    or they are immune to the spell entirely.  Another spell of the
    same type is 'power word blind'.


#
"SPELL REFRESH"
    Castable by :  mage 6, cleric 3, druid 4, sorcerer 6, necromancer 5
    Usage       :  cast 'refresh' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    A very useful spell, able to be cast be many different classes, it
    allows a tired target to continue travelling and fighting.  This
    spell is similar to 'second wind', just less useful and efficient,
    but is castable at much lower levels.  Casting this spell will
    recover an amount of move based on the power of the caster.


#
"SPELL REINCARNATE"
    Castable by :  druid 39
    Usage       :  cast 'reincarnate' <corpse obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    One of the most powerful spells in the realm, the druid can bring
    a deceased person back to life, but it may not be to the life they
    are accustomed.  This spell, which can only be cast outdoors in a
    forest, can also only be cast on the corpse of an adventurer.
    When cast, the druid will be reduced to near death, and weakened
    of all magical ability.  But the adventurer will be brought back
    to life in a random form.  It could be as an elf, or a orc, or a
    giant, or of many other possibilities.  There is no way to control
    the form chosen.  The newly reincarnated adventurer will be weaker
    after the ordeal for all time, his or her constitution taking a
    permanent penalty.

    Technical Details:  After dying, the player who is being reincarnated
    must *NOT* enter the game, they *MUST* remain at the menu screen.  Do
    *NOT* hit 1 to re-enter the game, stay at the menu until you are
    returned to the game automatically.


#
"SPELL REMOVE CURSE"
    Castable by :  cleric 8
    Usage       :  cast 'remove curse' <mob> | <obj>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Obj in Room
                   Obj in Inventory
                   Obj Equipped
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell is the only way, short of dying, of divesting oneself
    of cursed items.  Casting this spell allows a cursed object to
    be handled normally.  A player can 'remove', 'drop', 'put', 'get',
    donate, and 'junk' a formerly cursed item just like any other item.
    If casting the spell on another creature, it will remove the effects
    of the 'curse' spell and if they have a cursed object worn or wielded
    the spell will remove the curse on that object.  If the object is in
    the inventory of the caster, or on the ground, the object must be
    targeted.  For objects that are cursed, but can not worn or wielded
    by another creature, a spell scroll created by a cleric using 'scribe'
    can be recited by that creature on the object.

    Usage       :  cast 'remove paralysis' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent

"SPELL REMOVE POISON"
    Castable by :  cleric 17, druid 8, paladin 40, ranger 20
    Usage       :  cast 'remove poison' <mob> | <food/drink obj>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Obj in Room
                   Obj in Inventory
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell can cure a target creature whose blood burns with
    poison.  Successfully casting this spell will purge the target
    of all poison, no matter how long the poison was supposed to
    last.  Casting this spell on a piece of food or on a drink
    container will make the item safe to eat and drink.


#
"SPELL RESURRECTION"
    Castable by :  cleric 36
    Usage       :  cast 'resurrection' <corpse obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  33
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell can be cast on any corpse, whether an adventurer or
    a former opponent.  If cast on a former opponent, the corpse
    will rise and serve you, for the cost of 25000 gold. Be careful,
    if the creature has magical protections or was too powerful in
    life, it will rise from the dead, but refuse to serve you.  They
    will follow the caster for a period of time determined by the
    charisma of the caster.  If cast on a fellow adventurer, this
    spell costs the caster 75000 gold coins, and drains the caster of
    almost all health, magic, and stamina.  The victim will also be
    drained similarly, and will lose some of their constitution.

    Technical Details:  After dying, the player who is being reincarnated
    must leave the game entirely. Disconnect from the mud completely.  Do
    not remain at the menu screen, do not re-enter the game.  The best
    thing to do is to exit the game (hit 0 at the menu screen), and log
    in with a different character to watch and make sure you get
    resurrected.  After successfully resurrection, you can log back in
    with that character.


#
"SPELL SANCTUARY"
    Castable by :  cleric 26
    Usage       :  cast 'sanctuary' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    The workhorse of the cleric's arsenal, this spell is a must have
    tool for any adventuring party.  Calling on the gods to protect
    the target, it creates a nimbus of white light, that blunts any
    and all attacks against the individual.  When benefiting from
    this spell, the target suffers only 1/2 damage from any attack,
    even magical attacks.  Only a few rare psionic attacks are not
    affected by this spell.  The spell lasts only a few hours, not
    even a handful, but during that time, the gods protect the target.

"SPELL SCARE"
    Castable by :  mage 4, sorcerer 4
    Usage       :  cast 'scare' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -

    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A basic spell, of only limited use, it forces a very weak target
    to flee from the caster.  Basically a burst of fear, powered by
    magical energy, causes the target to run away, but immediately
    afterwards, they return to normal, and will remember what happened.


#
"SPELL SCOURGE OF THE WARLOCK"
    Castable by :  necromancer 29
    Usage       :  cast 'scourge of the warlock' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  Level d9
    Damage Type :  Poison
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  35
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    The darkest devotion of the minions of darkness, this spell is
    involves accepting a token of the Dark Lord.  Worn on the eyes,
    it is a mask, made of a magically created forked tongue.  So,
    the first time you cast this spell, you must not be wearing any
    object on your eyes, or else the spell will fail.  The tongue
    might have a special boon, granted by the Dark Lord, but it
    allows the scourge to be cast.  The scourge will poison the
    target, and then burn out most of the poison immediately,
    causing great damage, the scourge will leave lingering
    traces of poison in the veins, much like the 'poison' spell.

"SPELL SECOND WIND"
    Castable by :  mage 20, cleric 9, druid 14, sorcerer 20, paladin 35,

    will make the target less tired, and can be cast during combat.  Once

"SPELL SENSE LIFE"
    Castable by :  cleric 4
    Usage       :  cast 'sense life' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell is the only way of noticing a hidden creature in the room
    with you.  A hidden creature will reveal itself as a life form, but
    without the spell 'true sight', you will not be able to target the
    creature.  You will only know that something is there, not what
    the name of that something is.  This spell can last an incredibly
    long time when cast by a high level cleric, there have been cases
    of the spell lasting more than 10 days.


#
"SPELL SHADOW STEP"
    Castable by :  necromancer 20
    Usage       :  cast 'shadow step'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell allows a necromancer to use the shadows to remove
    him or herself from combat instantly and safely.  When this
    spell is cast, the necromancer will be transported into an
    adjacent room, provided that room is relatively safe.  A quick
    duck into the shadows, emerging nearby, it is an alternative
    to fleeing like a common fighter.


#
"SPELL SHIELD"
    Castable by :  mage 1, sorcerer 1
    Usage       :  cast 'shield' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  1
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    One of the simplest magical spells, this provides a perfect
    defense against the spell 'magic missile'.  It also provides
    a small level of protection against physical attacks by slightly
    stiffening the air around the caster.  The spell lasts for a
    period of time determined by the power of the caster.


#
"SPELL SHILLELAGH"
    Castable by :  druid 3
    Usage       :  cast 'shillelagh' <club obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in Inventory
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell can take a plain club and change it into a magical
    version called a shillelagh.  This only works on non-magical
    clubs, but it is permanent.  It does not create anything
    incredibly powerful, nor does it improve as the caster gets
    more powerful, but it might be handy in times of need.


#
"SPELL SHOCKING GRASP"
    Castable by :  mage 2, sorcerer 2
    Usage       :  cast 'shocking grasp' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  1-8 + Level
    Damage Type :  Electricity
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This requires that the caster touches the target, but if he
    or she does, this spell can zap the victim pretty good.  The
    mage builds up a large amount of magical energy, and then
    transforms it into electricity as he touches the target.  The
    resulting shock is enough to stop a heart.  Or start one.


#
"SPELL SILENCE"
    Castable by :  mage 21, cleric 23, druid 25, sorcerer 21
    Usage       :  cast 'silence' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Immensely Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    The bane of spell throwers everywhere, this spell makes the
    target unable to make any sound.  If the target doesn't
    manage to shake off the effect, no spells can be cast,
    no words can be spoken until the spell wears off, which
    is dependent on the power of the caster.


#
"SPELL SIPHON STRENGTH"
    Castable by :  necromancer 8
    Usage       :  cast 'siphon strength' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell strips the strength from the target and gives it
    to the necromancer caster.  The amount of strength taken is
    somewhat random, determined by the will of the victim to
    resist the dark magic.  The spell lasts for about a third
    of a day, at which time the victim gets his or her strength
    back.  The spell can not target fellow adventurers.


#
"SPELL SLEEP"
    Castable by :  mage 3, sorcerer 3
    Usage       :  cast 'sleep' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    By casting this spell, the magic user forces the target to
    suddenly become tired and fall asleep.  The target can
    resist the effects, and will know what the mage attempted
    to do.


#
"SPELL SLOWNESS"
    Castable by :  mage 19, sorcerer 19
    Usage       :  cast 'slowness' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    The opposite of the spell 'haste', this spell will cause the
    target to move about half as fast as normal.  It is especially
    noticeable in combat, when the opponent only gets about half
    as many attacks.  The duration of this effect is about a double
    handful of hours, which can feel like twice as long to the
    victim.


#
"SPELL SLOW POISON"
    Castable by :  druid 6, paladin 10, ranger 10
    Usage       :  cast 'slow poison' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell, which lasts a full day, will severely reduce the
    damage caused by being poisoned.  While a 'remove poison'
    would be better, this can help to keep the victim alive until
    the appropriate remedy can be found.


#
"SPELL SNARE"
    Castable by :  druid 8, ranger 5
    Usage       :  cast 'snare' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This interesting spell can only be cast in the outdoors,
    specifically in a forest.  But if those criteria are met
    the druid or ranger can attempt to convince Nature to
    help them in their fight.  Vines and supple bushes will
    reach towards the target.  If he or she doesn't evade
    them, they will instantly reduce their move down to
    zero, unable to walk, flee, and soon unable to fight at
    all.  As soon as the victim regains some move, they are
    able to break free of the vines easily.


#
"SPELL SOUL STEAL"
    Castable by :  necromancer 27
    Usage       :  cast 'soul steal' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell is amazing, and makes a necromancer very powerful.
    By reaching into the soul of a target with his dark magics,
    the necromancer can grab ahold of the magical essence of the
    target, and pull it out.  Once that has happened, he can
    absorb it for his own use, replenishing his own magical
    reservoir.  The amount stripped is random, but usually is
    enough to at least pay the caster back for the cost of the
    'soul steal' spell.  Sometimes it is enough to power expensive
    spells.  The amount is dictated by the strength of the target's
    will to hold on to their mana.


#
"SPELL SPEAK WITH PLANTS"
    Castable by :  druid 7
    Usage       :  cast 'speak with plants' <tree obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This minor spell doesn't have much use, except when taken
    into conjunction with the spell 'plant gate'.  Since
    the spell 'plant gate' requires a druid to know the given
    name of a tree, this spell can be used to help the druid
    to discover the names of any tree he or she runs across.
    Only trees can be talked to this way, and they usually
    don't have too much to say.


#
"SPELL SPECTRAL SHIELD"
    Castable by :  necromancer 4
    Usage       :  cast 'spectral shield'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Somewhat Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This minor spell creates a ghostly suit of armor that forms
    just over the current armor of the necromancer.  It is light
    enough to not hinder the caster at all, but it also does not
    give much protection.  It lasts longer if cast by a more
    powerful necromancer, potentially more than two days at the
    height of mortal power.


#
"SPELL STONE SKIN"
    Castable by :  mage 26, sorcerer 26, necromancer 32
    Usage       :  cast 'stone skin'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  40
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A powerful defensive spell available to some spell casters,
    this enables the caster to magically reinforce his or her
    skin.  While not truly turning the skin to stone, it takes
    on some of the color and properties of stone, and makes it
    much harder for enemies to successfully hit the caster.
    As a side benefit, this also gives the caster some
    resistance against stabbing and piercing attacks.  It
    should reduce the damage by these types of attacks by
    one half.  The duration of the effect is governed strictly
    by the power of the caster.


#
"SPELL STRENGTH"
    Castable by :  mage 6, sorcerer 6
    Usage       :  cast 'strength' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    A surprisingly simple transformation of magical energy into
    chemical energy allows the magic user to make a creature
    physically stronger.  The period of time is determined by
    the power of the caster.  The actual gain of strength is
    determined somewhat by what kind of role the target is
    involved in.  For instance, warrior types can receive
    a bigger strength boost than a mage.


#
"SPELL SUCCOR"
    Castable by :  mage 24, cleric 23, sorcerer 24
    Usage       :  cast 'succor'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Casting this spell brings a scroll into being.  The scroll
    is a simple one, containing the few magical syllables needed
    to cast the spell 'word of recall'.  Another person could
    then 'recite' the scroll to feel the effects of the 'word of
    recall' spell.

#
"SPELL SUIT OF BONE"
    Castable by :  necromancer 3
    Usage       :  cast 'suit of bone'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell basically creates magically strengthened bones
    from the darkness, and uses them to reinforce the existing
    armor of the caster.  The bones usually match the armor,
    so that a rib cage will form over the breastplate, and
    a femur over the leggings, etc.  The protection provided
    by this spell is a nice benefit, at least twice as much
    as provided by 'spectral shield'.  The bones stay in place
    for a full day after casting.


#
"SPELL SUMMON"
    Castable by :  mage 27, cleric 19, sorcerer 27
    Usage       :  cast 'summon' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in World
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This useful spell is a very popular utility spell.  By
    casting this with a fellow adventurer as the target, the
    target is immediately brought to your location.  There is
    no failure, except to fail the spell normally, through losing
    concentration.  However, it can also be used to bring an
    unwilling target, like a monster.  If that is the case, then
    the target receives the chance to resist the spell.  There
    are many conditions regarding the summoning of creatures.
    They must be on the same plane of existence as you.  If either
    you or the target are in a peaceful room, like the Reception,
    then summoning is impossible.  If you are underwater, or
    floating in mid-air, summoning isn't possible, you must have
    contact with the ground to send out the questing magic.  If
    the target is more than mortal, then summoning is impossible.
    If you are in a constricted space, then it is impossible to
    summon another person to it.  If the target is fighting, then
    they can not be summoned from the combat.  If the room they
    are in is magically protected, or the room you are in is
    magically protected, you can not summon the target.
    Rarely, the gods decide to make the planes shift and swirls,
    which also means that any extra-dimensional travel is
    impossible.  Despite all these restrictions, this is still
    a very useful spell, which can save a lot of time.


#
"SPELL SUNRAY"
    Castable by :  druid 27
    Usage       :  cast 'sunray' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  Special
    Damage Type :  Energy
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell has several effects, but the most deadly is
    reserved for undead monsters.  A blazing shaft of sunlight
    streams from above, bathing all in the room.  Any person
    not allied with the caster has a chance to be temporarily
    blinded by the spell.  If a creature is wearing equipment
    that doesn't tolerate sunlight, like drow equipment, then
    the equipment will likely be destroyed by the sunray.
    Finally, if the creature is undead or something like a
    myconoid, then it will take anywhere from 6 through 48
    points of damage.  The creature targeted by the spell
    will likely take more damage than those on the periphery
    of the sunray.


#
"SPELL TELEPORT"
    Castable by :  mage 17, sorcerer 17
    Usage       :  cast 'teleport' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  33
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Fairly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell can be a last ditch effort to avoid death.  Not
    recommended unless no other options present themselves.  By
    casting this spell the magic user sends a jolt of magical
    energy into the immediate world around him or her.  The end
    result of that jolt is to displace the caster from his or her
    location and allow the magic to carry him or her away to
    some other location.  The location is completely random, it
    can be anywhere on the same plane of existence, as long as
    no magical or natural barriers exist to prevent the
    translocation.  While that guarantees not ending up
    materializing inside of a boulder, it does not mean that you
    won't end up in the air above a ravine, or landing in the
    midst of a ravenous pack of wolves.  The fact that this
    spell can be cast in combat means that you might save yourself
    an agonizing death.  However, you also might jump from the
    frying pan into the fire.  If it is cast on another being,
    that being can resist the displacement effect of the jolt,
    and remain in the same location.


#
"SPELL TELEPORT WITHOUT ERROR"
    Castable by :  mage 30, sorcerer 30, necromancer 35
    Usage       :  cast 'teleport without error' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in World
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This powerful dimensional magic allows the caster to send any
    creature to the astral plane.  Anybody who is grouped with
    the target is also shifted to the astral plane.  In the
    astral plane, travel throughout the world is possible by
    entering the color pools, but blindly jumping into pools is
    not recommended for the wise adventurer.  Only grouped
    individuals can be sent, if you cast this spell and the
    target does not get shifted to the other plane, check to
    make sure the target is grouped, even if only with him or
    herself.


#
"SPELL TRACE CORPSE"
    Castable by :  necromancer 11
    Usage       :  cast 'trace corpse' <corpse obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in World
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    An odd spell, that shows just how closely necromancers are
    linked to death, 'trace corpse' allows the caster to gain
    information about any recent corpse.  If possible, the
    caster will actually be able to see the place where the
    corpse now lies.


#
"SPELL TRANSPORT VIA PLANT"
    Castable by :  druid 10
    Usage       :  cast 'transport via plant' <tree obj>
    Targets     :  Obj in World
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Similar to 'plant gate', this spell allows the druid to
    teleport him or herself from one tree to another tree.
    If the druid is standing in the same room with one of
    the many trees spread across the realm, he can name a
    target tree in casting this spell and be instantly
    transported to that tree.  There is no particular limit
    to this spell, the trees can even be on separate planes,
    and it is not considered multi-dimensional travel, so
    that when the planes are fuzzy and shifted, the druid
    can still travel.  The names of the trees of the realms
    is a closely guarded druid secret, but it is widely
    rumored that the name of the Karsinya tree in Market
    Square is called Tiberius.


#
"SPELL TRAVELLING"
    Castable by :  druid 10, ranger 15
    Usage       :  cast 'travelling' Self Only
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  2
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    An alternative to having to fly everywhere, this spell gives
    the druid or ranger the ability to travel easily over even
    the most difficult of outdoor terrain.  While remaining
    on the ground, this spell allows the druid or ranger to
    move as though they were walking across a level, easy path.
    While others may tire quickly while walking through mountains,
    the caster of this spell feels only as tired as though he
    were walking inside a hallway of a building.


#
"SPELL TREE"
    Castable by :  druid 15
    Usage       :  cast 'tree'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Truly demonstrating the affinity with nature that a druid
    possesses, this spell allows the druid to transform his
    very body into an actual tree.  The power of the druid
    directly corresponds to the power of the tree form.  And
    the tree is of course ambulatory, usually with a lot of
    attacks and a high resistance to damage.  The druid
    can return to his or her own form immediately by using
    the command 'return'.


#
"SPELL TREE TRAVEL"
    Castable by :  druid 8
    Usage       :  cast 'tree travel'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  2
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell is oddly named, but it's effect is simple.  Casting
    'tree travel' actually results in becoming slightly closer to
    nature than normal.  The effect of this is to give the caster
    a small edge in detecting dangers in combat, making them a
    little harder to hit.  The spell lasts for a full day, and
    costs little in terms of magical power, so most wise druids
    will maintain it constantly.


#
"SPELL TRUE SIGHT"
    Castable by :  cleric 19, druid 24
    Usage       :  cast 'true sight' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    This spell is a great boon to the target.  Essentially
    this spell means that nothing is obscured from the target.
    Being under the effect of this spell means that they can
    see invisible creatures, see in the dark, and it protects
    against heat sources from blinding creatures with
    infravision.  However, it does not protect against being
    blinded.  A creature who is under the effect of this spell
    and the spell 'sense life' will be able to target hidden
    creatures by name.


#
"SPELL TURN"
    Castable by :  cleric 1, druid 12, paladin 10
    Usage       :  cast 'turn' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell gives the cleric, druid, or paladin the
    power to make an undead creature flee the area.  The
    caster must be more powerful than the target, if the
    caster is significantly more powerful than the target,
    then the victim is far more likely to succumb to the
    spell.


#
"SPELL UNHOLY WORD"
    Castable by :
    Usage       :  cast 'unholy word'
    Targets     :  All Mobs in Room
    Damage      :  Special
    Damage Type :  Pure
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Immensely Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A powerful word, filled with the unholy might of the gods can
    render weaker creatures helpless, or even dead.  Depending
    on the power of the victims, they will either be struck dead,
    paralyzed, blinded, or stunned for a short time.  However,
    if they are too powerful, they will not be effected at all.
    This is the spell to use against good creatures, unlike it's
    twin, 'holy word', which is used against evil creatures.


#
"SPELL UNSUMMON"
    Castable by :  necromancer 7
    Usage       :  cast 'unsummon' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Slightly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell is very useful to a necromancer, especially one
    that uses his mastery of the undead to make many followers.
    By casting this spell on an undead follower, the necromancer
    can use the dark power that animates the dead to heal himself
    and to recover magical energy.  The amount of healing is
    random, but should be between 6 and 27 points of damage and
    he can regain a similar amount of mana.  A clever necromancer
    will become excellent at this spell and at the spell 'animate
    dead'.

#
"SPELL VAMPIRIC EMBRACE"
    Castable by :  necromancer 41
    Usage       :  cast 'vampiric embrace'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  Special
    Damage Type :  Drain
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell for 1/2 Damage
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  50
    Casting Time:  Slow
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Casting this spell allows the caster to gather and shape
    the dark energies that sustain the necromancer.  Molding
    it to his weapon, or to his own hands, it allows the
    necromancer to create a life sucking nimbus that can
    steal health from opponents struck by the necromancer.
    The health will be gathered by the necromancer, healing
    him or her of wounds.  There is only a chance of the
    nimbus successfully stealing from the opponent, but when
    it does, it could heal anywhere from 3 to 24 points of
    damage, unless the victim manages to resist the effect.


#
"SPELL VEGETABLE GROWTH"
    Castable by :  druid 20
    Usage       :  cast 'vegetable growth' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Not Self
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell can make a plant creature grow to twice it's natural size,
    but only in naturally occurring plants.  A polymorphed creature
    can not be targeted by this spell.  The creature has to be
    significantly weaker than the caster, stronger creatures shrug
    off the effects of the magic, which grants greater stamina and
    strength.  The animal will obey any 'order' of the caster.


#
"SPELL VENTRILOQUATE"
    Castable by :  mage 1, sorcerer 1
    Usage       :  cast 'ventriloquate' <mob> | <obj> <message>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Obj in Room
                   Not Self
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Not Fool A Person
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This fun spell can be used to make it seem as though another
    person or an object says the chosen message.  Everybody in
    the room gets a chance to check to see if they were fooled, so
    it is unlikely to fool a large group of people.  If a person
    doesn't succeed in seeing through the ruse, it will seem as
    though the target person or object actually said the message.


#
"SPELL WARP WEAPON"
    Castable by :  druid 19
    Usage       :  cast 'warp weapon' [<mob> | <obj>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   Obj in Room
                   Obj in Inventory
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  20
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Fairly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    A spell that can result in scraps of equipment littering the
    ground,  Casting this spell on an object will twist and
    warp the object, making it less sturdy, eventually the object
    will be destroyed, although it might take a few castings.
    If the target is a creature, then if the creature is wielding
    a weapon, this spell will attempt to destroy that weapon.


#
"SPELL WATER BREATH"
    Castable by :  mage 9, druid 6, sorcerer 9, ranger 17
    Usage       :  cast 'water breath' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  15
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    Casting this spell gives the target the ability to breath
    underwater for a period of time.  How long that period is
    depends on the power of the caster, a very powerful caster
    could give someone this ability for more than two days.
    This allows for exploration of underwater areas, but when
    the spell runs out, it would be a good idea to be in a room
    where there is air to breathe.


#
"SPELL WATER SERVANT"
    Castable by :  druid 37
    Usage       :  cast 'water servant'
    Targets     :  None
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  30
    Casting Time:  Medium
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This elemental summoning spell brings a servant from the
    plane of water.  The spell must be cast outdoors, and it
    can't be cast more than once per day.  Using 'order',
    the caster can command this powerful entity, but only for
    a full day, after that the water servant will regain it's
    own will.


#
"SPELL WEAKNESS"
    Castable by :  mage 6, sorcerer 6, necromancer 9
    Usage       :  cast 'weakness' [<mob>]
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
                   If Fighting: Automatically Target Opponent
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Spell to Negate
    Aggressive  :  Yes
    Mana Cost   :  10
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  No
    Difficulty  :  Moderate
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    Casting this spell will make the target suffer a sudden
    bout of weakness.  Equipment will be heavier, it will
    be harder to swing a weapon, in general the target will
    be very unhappy.  The amount of strength drained is
    dependent on the power of the caster.  The duration
    is also determined by the power of the caster, high
    level casters can make this condition last over a day.


#
"SPELL WEB"
    Castable by :  mage 11, sorcerer 11
    Usage       :  cast 'web' <mob>
    Targets     :  Mob in Room
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  vs. Paralyzation to Negate
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  3
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  Yes
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Slightly Difficult
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    With a wave of a hand, the magic user can cause
    a huge sticky web to appear, surrounding a target.
    Casting this spell will make fighting and movement
    much more difficult for the target.  There are
    many factors which come into how well this spell
    works, such as the race of the target, how big
    the target is, and whether it is cast indoors, or
    outdoors.  It is more effective indoors, due to the
    limited space and more surfaces for the web to
    grab on to.

"SPELL WIZARDEYE"
    Castable by :  mage 35, sorcerer 35
    Usage       :  cast 'wizard eye'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -

    Saving Throw:  -

    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    the mage can create a disembodied eyeball.  This spell
    lasts only for a few hours, but during that time
    the magic user is able to use the eye to scout out the
    adjacent rooms by looking in the direction they wish to
    view.


#
"SPELL WORD OF RECALL"
    Castable by :  cleric 15
    Usage       :  cast 'word of recall'
    Targets     :  Self Only
    Damage      :  -
    Damage Type :  -
    Saving Throw:  -
    Aggressive  :  No
    Mana Cost   :  5
    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  Yes

    Every adventurer has someplace that they consider "home".
    Usually it's the place where they last rented a room to
    sleep.  This spell will return the caster to wherever
    this place is, instantly, as long as they are on the
    same plane as the location.  The gods grant this ability,
    but they do not allow it to be used as a form of
    cowardice, so you must not be fighting when attempting
    to cast this spell.

"SPELL WRATH OF GOD"
    Castable by :

    Casting Time:  Fast
    Combat Cast :  No
    Accumulative:  Yes
    Difficulty  :  Very Easy
    Scribe/Brew :  No

    This spell calls down the smiting power of the gods on the
    head of the target.  A devastating attack, that can only
    be partially avoided, no creature is completely immune,
    except those of godly nature.


#
"TERM AC"

    This refers to 'Armor Class', the term used to describe
    how well protected from physical attacks a person is.
    Your general level of protection can be determined from
    the 'attribute' command.

    barely armored
    Lightly armored
    Medium-armored
    Fairly well armored
    Well armored
    Quite well armored
    Very well armored
    Extremely well armored
    armored like a Dragon

#
"TERM ADVENTURER"

    This term refers to a mid level mortal, who is just beginning
    to understand some of the keys to gaining great mortal power.  There
    are a group of distinctions that can help to narrow down how powerful
    an adventurer is.

    Apprentice
    Pilgrim
    Explorer
    Adventurer
    Mystical
    Hero

#
"TERM AGING"

    Most adventurers only dream of living to a ripe old age,
    but the effects of living past the bloom of your youth
    are not all bad.  While you lose some vitality and health,
    your mental facilities actually improve, giving you a
    greater ability to regenerate magical energy.    

#
"TERM ALIGN"

    This refers to 'alignment', the term used to describe
    the type of life choices a person makes.  Generally,
    it falls into three categories:  good, neutral, evil.
    Creatures of good alignment are generally unselfish,
    giving, and righteous.  Creatures of evil alignment tend
    to be selfish, corrupt, and greedy.  Those who fall into
    the middle are considered neutral.  Killing evil makes
    you good, killing good makes you evil.  Killing neutral
    moves you towards neutrality.  The 'score' command can
    help to determine where you fall on the alignment scale.

    Lawful Good
    Neutral Good
    Chaotic Good
    Lawful Neutral
    True Neutral
    Chaotic Neutral
    Lawful Evil
    Neutral Evil
    Chaotic Evil

#
"TERM ALIGNMENT"

    This is the term used to describe the type of life
    choices a person makes.  Generally, it falls into
    three categories:  good, neutral, evil.  Creatures of
    good alignment are generally unselfish, giving, and
    righteous.  Creatures of evil alignment tend to be
    selfish, corrupt, and greedy.  Those who fall into
    the middle are considered neutral.  Killing evil makes
    you good, killing good makes you evil.  Killing neutral
    moves you towards neutrality.  The 'score' command can
    help to determine where you fall on the alignment scale.

    Lawful Good
    Neutral Good
    Chaotic Good
    Lawful Neutral
    True Neutral
    Chaotic Neutral
    Lawful Evil
    Neutral Evil
    Chaotic Evil

#
"TERM APPRENTICE"

    This term refers to a low level mortal, who is just starting on their
    road to fame and adventure in the quest for great mortal power.  There
    are a group of distinctions that can help to narrow down how powerful
    an adventurer is.

    Apprentice
    Pilgrim
    Explorer
    Adventurer
    Mystical
    Hero

#
"TERM AREA EFFECT"

    This is the term used to describe skills or spells that
    affect more than a single target in a room.  Some spells
    and skills can affect a limited number of creatures, and
    some can affect every creature.  Spells such as 'fireball'
    and 'earthquake' are examples of this.

#
"TERM ARMOR CLASS"

    This refers to the term used to describe how well protected
    from physical attacks a person is.  Your general level of
    protection can be determined from the 'attribute' command.

    barely armored
    Lightly armored
    Medium-armored
    Fairly well armored
    Well armored
    Quite well armored
    Very well armored
    Extremely well armored
    armored like a Dragon

#
"TERM ARMOR"

    This term can refer to several things.  In regards to
    equipment, it can describe what type of equipment an
    object is.  That an object is armor rather than a weapon
    or a wand.  It can also refer to the spell 'armor'.  In
    regards to the 'stats' of an item, it can be used to
    describe a magical effect of an item, to improve or
    worsen the 'armor class' of the wearer.  A negative
    value indicates better protection, a positive value
    indicates that the item will make you easier to be hit
    in combat.

#
"TERM BANNING"

    This term refers to the worst punishment available to the
    implementors of the mud.  Being banned means that all of
    a player's characters are destroyed and he or she is denied
    from logging into the mud.  This punishment is only reserved
    for gross, unforgivable offenses against the mud.

#
"TERM BB"

    This term refers to the spell 'blade barrier'.  If you hear
    that a mob is "bb'd" the speaker is referring to the idea
    that the mob is protected by the 'blade barrier' spell.

#
"TERM BOARD"

    This term refers to the fact that certain objects can act
    as bulletin boards to post messages on.  The one that is
    most commonly used by mortals is found in the Adventurers
    Lodge, which is just east and north of Meeting Square in
    'Karsinya'.

#
"TERM CHA"

    This term refers to 'charisma', which is a 'stat' that
    describes the comeliness and force of personality of
    a creature.  A high 'charisma' can mean that a person
    is likable and good looking.  A low 'charisma' means
    that the person is generally unpleasant to be around.
    This can make a difference in how shopkeepers react
    to you and how long charmed individuals will follow
    you.  The 'attribute' command gives information on
    all of your 'stats'.

#
"TERM CHARISMA"

    This term refers to the 'stat' that describes the
    comeliness and force of personality of a creature.
    A high 'charisma' can mean that a person is likable
    and good looking.  A low 'charisma' means that
    the person is generally unpleasant to be around.
    This can make a difference in how shopkeepers react
    to you and how long charmed individuals will follow
    you.  The 'attribute' command gives information on
    all of your 'stats'.

#
"TERM CHR"

    This term refers to 'charisma', which is a 'stat' that
    describes the comeliness and force of personality of
    a creature.  A high 'charisma' can mean that a person
    is likable and good looking.  A low 'charisma' means
    that the person is generally unpleasant to be around.
    This can make a difference in how shopkeepers react
    to you and how long charmed individuals will follow
    you.  The 'attribute' command gives information on
    all of your 'stats'.

#
"TERM CLAN"

    This term refers to a player run organization of mortals
    that promotes a level of camaraderie between it's members.
    Each clan has it's own roster, which is controlled by
    the leader of the clan.  The specific application
    process for each clan is governed by that clan, the
    immortals tend to have no particular role in a clan,
    except in setting up new clans or erasing defunct
    clans.  A clan is usually guided by some principle,
    and clan members have their own communication methods
    and places to meet, called clanhalls.

#
"TERM CON"

    This term refers to 'constitution', which is a 'stat'
    that describes the hardiness of a creature.  A high
    'constitution' means that a creature is likely to
    have more hitpoints than a creature with a low
    constitution.  The 'attribute' command gives information
    on all of your 'stats'.

#
"TERM CONSTITUTION"

    This term refers the 'stat' that describes the
    hardiness of a creature.  A high 'constitution'
    means that a creature is likely to have more
    hitpoints than a creature with a low constitution.
    The 'attribute' command gives information on
    all of your 'stats'.

#
"TERM CORPSE RETRIEVAL"

    This term refers to the actions that can be taken
    after somebody dies.  Since all of the equipment
    and the corpse of the recently deceased are still
    in the room with the creature that killed them, a
    corpse retrieval can be requested of the other
    players on the mud.  It usually means that a party
    of adventurers go to the place of death and kill
    the mob that killed the adventurer, and guard the
    corpse until the person returns for their equipment.

#
"TERM CR"

    This term refers to 'corpse retrieval', which are
    the actions that can be taken after somebody dies.
    Since all of the equipment and the corpse of the
    recently deceased are still in the room with the
    creature that killed them, a corpse retrieval can
    be requested of the other players on the mud.  It
    usually means that a party of adventurers go to
    the place of death and kill the mob that killed
    the adventurer, and guard the corpse until the
    person returns for their equipment.

#
"TERM CS"

    This term refers to the spell 'chillshield'.  If you hear
    that a mob is "cs'd" the speaker is referring to the idea
    that the mob is protected by the 'chillshield' spell.

#
"TERM DAMAGE"

    This term is a generic way of referring to anything
    that reduces the 'hitpoints' of a 'mob'.  Most
    damage is of a certain type, such as fire or slashing.
    While rare, the non-type specific damage can be very
    useful, since an opponent may have resistances to
    many forms of "typed" damage.  However, the converse
    is true, some opponents will be susceptible to a
    particular type of damage.    

#
"TERM DAMROLL"

    This term refers to one of a couple related terms.  The
    first is to describe the magical property of increased
    damage granted to a weapon or piece of armor.  For instance
    you might say that "This amulet is +1 damroll".  The second
    is used to describe the overall sum of a creature's damroll.
    "What is your damroll?"  The general level of your damroll
    can be found using the 'attribute' command.

    Quite bad
    Pretty lousy
    Not Much of one
    Not bad
    Pretty good
    Damn good
    Very good
    Extremely good
    Magnificent

#
"TERM DEATH"

    This term refers to the fact that when reduced to
    negative 'hitpoints' your character will die.  On
    Havok, death is a temporary, but serious, setback.
    The order of the consequences of it happening are:
    
    A corpse of your body, with all your gear, is left
    in the spot where you died.  Your corpse and your
    gear is able to be picked up by anybody, even
    scavenging mobs.

    Your amount of experience is reduced, by up to
    half, making it that much harder to gain your
    next level.

    Returned to the main menu, similar to when you
    first log in.
    --
    
    When you are at the main menu, you have a 
    decision to make.  If you have a reason to
    expect the 'resurrection' spell or 'reincarnation'
    spell to be cast, you *SHOULD NOT RE-ENTER THE
    WORLD BY HITTING "1"*, doing so will make it
    impossible to cast either of the two spells.
    For 'reincarnation' you will be automatically
    returned to the game if you are waiting at the
    menu.  For 'resurrection' the best thing to do
    is to log off with the "deceased" character and
    log in with another character and wait until you 
    are resurrected before returning with the original
    character.  Since returning to the game prematurely
    will make these spells impossible, it is not
    recommended that you make your 'alias' 1 a command
    that you would spam in combat.  If you make "1" 
    equivalent to the 'flee' command, you might 
    accidently re-enter the game after dying when you
    really meant to 'flee'.
    --

    Once you have returned to the game, you will be:

    Returned to your last 'rent' inn.

    'Hitpoints' is set to 1.
    
    --
    
    At this point you should be careful about hurrying
    back to where you died.  Dying once is bad, dying
    twice in a row can be downright depressing.  It
    is acceptable to ask for help in what is usually
    termed a 'corpse retrieval' or 'CR'.

    It should be noted that if you die often enough,
    you can lose levels of experience.  Basically,
    dying multiple times quickly can reduce your
    total amount of experience to a point where
    the mud will strip you of your hard-earned
    levels.        
    
    While dying is not a pleasant thing, it is not
    the end of the world either.  Do not be overly
    discouraged, and it is never worth it to 'remake'
    a character just because of some dying.  It might
    feel differently, but you will have an easier time
    earning back the experience you lost with the
    higher level "dying" character than starting over
    with a level 1 character.
    
#
"TERM DEATH TRAP"

    This term refers to a room that has a special effect when
    entered by an adventurer.  Usually described as an
    inescapable situation that results in death, it acts
    like a minor form of death.  The hapless adventurer
    who stumbles into one of these rooms is returned instantly
    to the menu screen, and when they return to the game they
    will find themselves naked, without equipment of any kind.
    They will still have all of their experience, and all of
    their gold, but the equipment will be lost.  Some consider
    this a fate worse than death.

#
"TERM DEX"

    This term refers to 'dexterity' the 'stat' that describes
    how agile and quick a creature is.  A high 'dexterity'
    will make you harder to hit in battle as you are more
    skilled at dodging than a person with a low 'dexterity'.
    The 'attribute' command gives information on all
    of your 'stats'.

#
"TERM DEXTERITY"

    This term refers to the 'stat' that describes
    how agile and quick a creature is.  A high 'dexterity'
    will make you harder to hit in battle as you are more
    skilled at dodging than a person with a low 'dexterity'.
    The 'attribute' command gives information on all
    of your 'stats'.
